  <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

    <body>

      <div n="4" type="sthāna">

        <head>cikitsāsthānaṃ</head>

        <div n="1" type="adhyāya">
          <head>prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.1"> athāto dvivraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.3"> dvau vraṇau bhavataḥ śārīra, āgantuś ca | tayoḥ śārīraḥ
            pavanapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātanimittaḥ; āgantur api puruṣa<pc
              > </pc>paśu<pc> </pc>pakṣi<pc> </pc>vyāla<pc> </pc>sarīsṛpa<pc
              > </pc>prapatanapīḍana<pc> </pc>prahārāgnikṣāra<pc> </pc>viṣa<pc
              > </pc>tīkṣṇauṣadha<pc> </pc>śakala<pc
              > </pc>kapālaśṛṅgackreṣuparaśuśaktikuntādyāyudhābhighāta<pc> </pc>nimittaḥ |
            tatra tulye vraṇasāmānye dvikāraṇotthānaprayojanasāmarthyād dvivraṇīya ity
            ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.4"> sarvasminn evāgantuvraṇe tatkālam eva kṣatoṣmaṇaḥ
            prasṛtasyopaśamārthaṃ ceti śleṣmaśoṇitābhyāṃ, sphuraṇatodadāhadhūmāyanaprāyaḥ
            pītatanuraktasrāvī ceti vātapittaśoṇitebhyaḥ,
            kaṇḍūsphuraṇacumacumāyamānaprāyaḥ pāṇḍughanaraktāsrāvī ceti
            vātaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ, dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūprāyaḥ pāṇḍughanaraktāsrāvī ceti
            pittaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ, trividhavarṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ
            pavanapittakaphebhyaḥ,
            nirdahananirmathanasphuraṇatodadāhapākarāgakaṇḍūsvāpabahulo
            nānāvarṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ pavanapittakaphaśoṇitebhyaḥ, jihvātalābho
            mṛduḥ snigdhaḥ ślakṣṇo vigatavedanaḥ suvyavasthito nirāsrāvaś ceti śuddho
            vraṇa iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.5"> doṣopaplavaviśeṣaḥ punaḥ samāsataḥ pañcadaśaprakāraḥ,
            prasaraṇasāmarthyāt, yathokto vraṇapraśnādhikāre; śuddhatvāt ṣoḍaśaprakāra ity
            eke|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.6"> tasya lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ sāmānyaṃ, vaiśeṣikaṃ ca| tatra
            sāmānyaṃ ruk| vraṇa gātravicūrṇane, vraṇayatīti vraṇaḥ| viśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ
            punarvātādiliṅgaviśeṣaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.7"> tatra śyāvāruṇābhastanuḥ śītaḥ picchilo 'lpasrāvī
            rūkṣaścaṭacaṭāyanaśīlaḥ sphuraṇāyāmatodabhedavedanābahulo nirmāṃsaś ceti
            vātāt, kṣiprajaḥ pītanīlābhaḥ kiṃśukodakābhoṣṇasrāvī dāhapākarāgavikārakārī
            pītapiḍakājuṣṭaśceti pittāt, pratatacaṇḍakaṇḍūbahulaḥ sthūlauṣṭhaḥ
            stabdhasirāsnāyujālāvatataḥ kaṭhinaḥ pāṇḍvavabhāso mandavedanaḥ
            śuklaśītasāndrapicchilāsrāvī guruśceti kaphāt, pravāladalanicayaprakāśaḥ
            kṛṣṇasphoṭapiḍākājālopacitasturaṅgasthānagandhiḥ savedano dhūmāyanaśīlo
            raktasrāvī pittaliṅgaśceti raktāt, todadāhadhūmāyanaprāyaḥ
            pītāruṇābhastadvarṇasrāvī ceti vātapittābhyāṃ, kaṇḍūyanaśīlaḥ sanistodo rūkṣo
            gururdāruṇo muhurmuhuḥ śītapicchilālpasrāvī ceti vātaśleṣmabhyāṃ, guruḥ sadāha
            uṣṇaḥ pītapāṇḍusrāvī ceti pittaśleṣmabhyāṃ, rūkṣastanustodabahulaḥ supta iva
            ca raktāruṇābhastadvarṇāsrāvī ceti vātaśoṇitābhyāṃ, ghṛtamaṇḍābho
            mīnadhāvanatoyagandhirmṛdurvisarpyuṣṇakṛṣṇasrāvī ceti pittaśoṇitābhyāṃ, rakto
            guruḥ snigdhaḥ picchilaḥ kaṇḍūprāyaḥ sthiro saraktapāṇḍusrāvī ceti
            śleṣmaśoṇitābhyāṃ, sphuraṇatodadāhadhūmāyanaprāyaḥ pītatanuraktasrāvī ceti
            vātapittaśoṇitebhyaḥ, kaṇḍūsphuraṇacumacumāyamānaprāyaḥ pāṇḍughanaraktāsrāvī
            ceti vātaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ, dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūprāyaḥ pāṇḍughanaraktāsrāvī ceti
            pittaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ, trividhavarṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ
            pavanapittakaphebhyaḥ,
            nirdahananirmathanasphuraṇatodadāhapākarāgakaṇḍūsvāpabahulo
            nānāvarṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ pavanapittakaphaśoṇitebhyaḥ, jihvātalābho
            mṛduḥ snigdhaḥ ślakṣṇo vigatavedanaḥ suvyavasthito nirāsrāvaśceti śuddho vraṇa
            iti|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.8"> tasya vraṇasya paṣṭirupakramā bhavanti | tad yathā
            apatarpaṇam ālepaḥ pariṣeko 'bhyaṅgaḥ svedo vimpālanam upanāhaḥ pācanaṃ
            visrāvaṇaṃ sneho vamanaṃ virecanaṃ chedanaṃ bhedanaṃ dāraṇaṃ lekhanam eṣaṇam
            āharaṇaṃ vyadhanaṃ visrāvaṇaṃ sīvanaṃ sandhānaṃ pīḍanaṃ śoṇitāsthāpanaṃ
            nirvāpaṇam utkārikā kaṣāyo vartiḥ kalkaḥ sarpistailaṃ rasakriyā 'vacūrṇanaṃ
            vraṇadhūpanam utsādanam avasādanaṃ mṛdukarma dāruṇakarma kṣārakarmāgnikarma
            kṛṣṇakarma pāṇḍukarma pratisāraṇaṃ romasañjananaṃ lomāpaharaṇaṃ
            bastikarmottarabastikarma bandhaḥ patradānaṃ kṛmighnaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ viṣaghnaṃ
            śirovirecanaṃ nasyaṃ kavaladhāraṇaṃ dhūmo madhusārpir yantram āhāro
            rakṣāvidhānam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.9"> teṣu kaṣāyo vartiḥ kalkaḥ sarpistailaṃ rasakriyā
            'vacūrṇanam iti śodhanaropaṇāni, teṣv aṣṭau śastrakṛtyāḥ, śoṇitāsthāpanaṃ
            kṣāro 'gnir yantram ahāro rakṣāvidhānaṃ bandhavidhānaṃ coktāni,
            snehasvedanavamanavirecanabastyuttarabastiśirovirecananasyadhūmakavalaghāraṇānyanyatra
            vakṣyāmaḥ, yad anyad avaśiṣṭam upakramajātaṃ tad iha vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.10"> ṣaḍvidhaḥ prāgupadiṣṭaḥ śophaḥ, tasyaikādaśopakramā
            bhavanty apatarpaṇādayo virecanāntāḥ; te ca viśeṣeṇa śothapratīkāre vartante,
            vraṇabhāvam āpannasya ca na virudhyante; śeṣās tu prāyeṇa vraṇapratīkārahetava
            eva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.11"> apatarpaṇamādya upakramaḥ; eṣa sarvaśophānāṃ sāmānyaḥ
            pradhānatamaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.12"> bhavanti cātra doṣocchrāyopaśāntyarthaṃ doṣānaddhasya
            dehinaḥ | avekṣya doṣaṃ prāṇaṃ ca kāryaṃ syād apatarpaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.13"> ūrdhvamārutatṛṣṇākṣunmukhaśoṣaśramānvitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             na kāryaṃ garbhiṇīvṛddhabāladurbalabhīrubhiḥdhyāme sarakte vedanāvati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.14"> śopheṣūtthitamātreṣu vraṇeṣūgrarujeṣu ca|
            yathāsvairauṣadhairlepaṃ pratyekaśyena kārayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.15"> yathā pravajvalite veśmanyambhasā paribecanam| kṣipraṃ
            praśamayatyagnimevam ālepanaṃ rujaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.16"> prahlādane śodhane ca śophasya haraṇe tathā| utsādane
            ropaṇe ca lepaḥ syāt tu tadarthakṛt|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.17"> vātaśophe tu vedanopaśamārthaṃ
            sarpistailadhānyāmlamāṃsarasavātaharauṣadhaniṣkvāthairaśītaiḥ pariṣekān
            kurvīta, pittaraktābhighātaviṣanimitteṣu
            kṣīraghṛtamadhuśarkarodakekṣurasamadhurauṣadhakṣīravṛkṣaniṣkvāthairanuṣṇaiḥ
            pariṣekān kurvīta, śleṣmaśophe tu
            tailamūtrakṣārodakasurāśuktakaphaghnauṣadhaniṣkvāthairaśītaiḥ pariṣekān
            kurvīta|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.18"> yathā+ambubhiḥ sicyamānaḥ śāntimagnirniyacchati|
            doṣāgnirevaṃ sahasā pariṣekeṇa śāmyati|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.19"> abhyaṅgas tu doṣamālokyopayukto doṣopaśamaṃ mṛdutāṃ ca
            karoti|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.20"> svedavimlāpanādīnāṃ kriyāṇāṃ prāk sa ucyate| pañcāt
            karmasu cādiṣṭaḥ sa ca visrāvaṇādiṣu|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.21"> rujāvatāṃ dāruṇānāṃ kaṭhinānāṃ tathaiva ca| śophānāṃ
            svedanaṃ kāryaṃ ye cāpy evaṃvidhā vraṇāḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.22"> sthirāṇāṃ rujatāṃ mandaṃ kāryaṃ vimlāpanaṃ bhavet|
            abhyajya svedayitvā tu veśunāḍyā tataḥ śanaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.23"> vimardayed bhiṣak prājñastalenāṅguṣṭhakena vā| śophayor
            upanāhaṃ tu kuryād āmavidagdhayoḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.24"> avidagdhaḥ śamaṃ yāti vidagdhaḥ pākameti ca| nivartate na
            yaḥ śopho virekāntair upakramaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.25"> tasya saṃpācanaṃ kuryāt samāhṛtyauṣadhāni tu|
            dadhitakrasurāśuktadhānyāmlairyojitāni tu|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.26"> snigdhāni lavaṇīkṛtya paced utkārikāṃ śubhām|
            sairaṇḍapatrayā śophaṃ nāhayed uṣṇayā tayā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.27"> hitaṃ sambhojanaṃ cāpi pākāyābhimukho yadi|
            vedanopaśamārthāya tathā pākaśamāya ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.28"> acirotpatite śophe kuryāc choṇitamokṣaṇam| saśophe
            kaṭhine dhyāme sarakte vedanāvati|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.29"> saṃrabdhe viṣame cāpi vraṇe visrāvaṇaṃ hitam |
            <caesura/>
             saviṣe ca viśeṣeṇa jalaukobhiḥ padais tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.30"> vedanāyāḥ praśāntyarthaṃ pākasyāprāptaye tathā |
            <caesura/>
             sopadravāṇāṃ rūkṣāṇāṃ kṛśānāṃ vraṇaśoṣiṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.31"> yathāsvamauṣadhaiḥ siddhaṃ snehapānaṃ vidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             utsannamāṃsaśophe tu kaphajuṣṭe viśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.32"> saṃkliṣṭaśyā(dhyā)marudhire vraṇe pracchardanaṃ hitam |
            <caesura/>
             vātapittapraduṣṭeṣu dīrghakālānubandhiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.33"> virecanaṃ praśaṃsanti vraṇeṣu vraṇakovidāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apākeṣu tu rogeṣu kaṭhineṣu sthireṣu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.34"> snāyukothādiṣu tathā cchedanaṃ prāptamucyate |
            <caesura/>
             antaḥpūyeṣv avaktreṣu tathaivotsaṅgavatsv api|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.35"> gatimatsu ca rogeṣu bhedanaṃ prāptam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             bālavṛddhāsahakṣīṇabhīrūṇāṃ yoṣitām api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.36"> marmopari ca jāteṣu rogeṣūkteṣu dāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             supakve piṇḍite śophe pīḍanair upapīḍite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.37"> pākodvṛtteṣu doṣeṣu tat tu kāryaṃ vijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             supiṣṭair dāraṇadravyair yuktaiḥ kṣāreṇa vā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.38"> kaṭhinān sthūlavṛttauṣṭhān dīryamāṇān punaḥ punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭhinotsannamāṃsāṃś ca lesvanenācared bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.39"> samaṃ likhet sulikhitaṃ likhenniravaśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vartmanāṃ tu pramāṇena samaṃ śastreṇa nirlikhet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.40"> kṣaumaṃ plotaṃ picuṃ phenaṃ yāvaśūkaṃ sasaindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             kakaśāni ca patrāṇi lekhanārthe pradāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.41"> nāḍīvraṇāñ śalyagarbhānunmārgyutsaṅginaḥ śanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             karīrabālāṅgulibhir eṣaṇyā vaiṣayed bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.42"> netravartmagudābhyāsanāḍyo 'vaktrāḥ saśoṇitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cuccūpodakajaiḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ karīrair eṣayet tu tāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.43"> saṃvṛtāsaṃvṛtāsyeṣu vraṇeṣu matimān bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             yathoktamāharecchalyaṃ prāptoddharaṇalakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.44"> roge vyadhanasādhye tu yathoddeśaṃ pramāṇataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śastraṃ nidadhyād doṣaṃ ca srāvayet kīrtitaṃ yathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.45"> apākopadrutā ye ca māṃsasthā vivṛtāṃś ca ye |
            <caesura/>
             yathoktaṃ sīvanaṃ teṣu kāryaṃ sandhānam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.46"> pūyagarbhānaṇudvārān vraṇānmarmagatānapi |
            <caesura/>
             yathoktaiḥ pīḍanadravyaiḥ samantāt paripīḍayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.47"> śuṣyamāṇamupekṣeta pradehaṃ pīḍanaṃ prati |
            <caesura/>
             na cābhimukhamālimpettathā doṣaḥ prasicyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.48"> tais tair nimittair bahudhā śoṇite prasrute bhṛśam |
            <caesura/>
             kāryaṃ yathoktaṃ vaidyena śoṇitāsthāpanaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.49"> dāhapākajvaravatāṃ vraṇānāṃ pittakopataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             raktena cābhibhūtānāṃ kāryaṃ nirvāpaṇaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.50"> yathoktaiḥ śītaladravyaiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭair ghṛtāplutaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dihyādabahalān sekān suśītāṃś cāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.51"> vraṇeṣu kṣīṇamāṃseṣu tanusrāviṣvapākiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             todakāṭhinyapāruṣyaśūlavepathumatsu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.52"> vātaghnavarge 'mlagaṇe kākolyādigaṇe tathā |
            <caesura/>
             snaihikeṣu ca bījeṣu paced utkārikāṃ śubhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.53"> teṣāṃ ca svedanaṃ kāryaṃ sthirāṇāṃ vedanāvatām |
            <caesura/>
             durgandhānāṃ kledavatāṃ picchilānāṃ viśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.54"> kaṣāyaiḥ śodhanaṃ kāryaṃ śodhanaiḥ prāgudīritaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             antaḥśalyānaṇumukhān gambhīrān māṃsasaṃśritān | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.55"> śodhanadravyayuktābhir vartibhis tān yathākramam ||
            <caesura/>
             pūtimāṃsapraticchannān mahādoṣāṃś ca śodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.56"> kalkīkṛtair yathālābhaṃ vartidravyaiḥ puroditaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittapraduṣṭān gambhīrān dāhapākaprapīḍitān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.57"> kārpāsīphalamiśreṇa jayec chodhanasarpiṣā |
            <caesura/>
             utsannamāṃsānasnigdhānalpasrāvān vraṇāṃs tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.58"> sarṣapasnehayuktena dhīmāṃstailena śodhayet |
            <caesura/>
             tailenāśudhyamānānāṃ śodhanīyāṃ rasakriyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.59"> vraṇānāṃ sthiramāṃsānāṃ kuryād dravyair udīritaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāye vidhivatteṣāṃ kṛte cādhiśrayet punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.60"> surāṣṭrajāṃ sakāsīsāṃ dadyāc cāpi manaḥśilām |
            <caesura/>
             haritālaṃ ca matimāṃstatastām avacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.61"> mātuluṅgarasopetāṃ sakṣaudrāmatimarditām |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇeṣu dattvā tāṃ tiṣṭhettrīṃstrīṃś ca divasān param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.62"> medojuṣṭānagambhīrān durgandhāṃś cūrṇaśodhanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             upācaret bhiṣak prājñaḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ śodhanavartijaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.63"> śuddhalakṣaṇayuktānāṃ kaṣāyaṃ ropaṇaṃ hitam |
            <caesura/>
             tatra kāryaṃ yathoddiṣṭair dravyair vaidyena jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.64"> avedanānāṃ śuddhānāṃ gambhīrāṇāṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             hitā ropaṇavartyaṅgakṛtā ropaṇavartayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.65"> apetapūtimāṃsānāṃ māṃsasthānāmarohatām |
            <caesura/>
             kalkaḥ saṃrohaṇaḥ kāryastilajo madhusṃyutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.66"> sa mādhuryāt tathauṣṇyāc ca snehāc cānilanāśanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyabhāvānmādhuryāttiktatvāc cāpi pittahṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.67"> auṣṇyāt kaṣāyabhāvāc ca tiktatvāc ca kaphe hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śodhayed ropayec cāpi yuktaḥ śodhanaropaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.68"> nimbapatramadhubhyāṃ tu yuktaḥ saṃśodhanaḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvābhyāṃ sarpiṣā cāpi yuktaś cāpy uparopaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.69"> tilavadyavakalkaṃ tu kecid āhur manīṣiṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śamayed avidagdhaṃ ca vidagdham api pācayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.70"> pakvaṃ bhinatti bhinnaṃ ca śodhayed ropayet tathā |
            <caesura/>
             pittaraktaviṣāgantūn gambhīrānapi ca vraṇān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.71"> ropayed ropaṇīyena kṣīrasiddhena sarpiṣā |
            <caesura/>
             kaphavātābhibhūtānāṃ vraṇānāṃ matimān bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.72"> kārayed ropaṇaṃ tailaṃ bheṣajais tad yathoditaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             abandhyānāṃ calasthānāṃ śuddhānāṃ ca praduṣyatām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.73"> dviharidrāyutāṃ kuryād ropaṇārthāṃ rasakriyām |
            <caesura/>
             samānāṃ sthiramāṃsānāṃ tvaksthānāṃ ropaṇaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.74"> cūrṇaṃ vidadhyānmatimān prāksthānokto vidhiryathā |
            <caesura/>
             śodhano ropaṇaś caiva vidhiryo 'yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.75"> sarvavraṇānāṃ sāmānyenokto doṣāviśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             eṣa āgamasiddhatvāt tathaiva phaladarśanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.76"> mantravat saṃprayoktavyo na mīmāṃsyaḥ kathañcana |
            <caesura/>
             svabuddhyā cāpi vibhajet kaṣāyādiṣu saptasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.77"> bheṣajāni yathāyogaṃ yānyuktāni purā mayā |
            <caesura/>
             ādye dve pañcamūlyau tu gaṇo yaś cānilāpahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.78"> sa vātaduṣṭe dātavyaḥ kaṣāyādiṣu saptasu |
            <caesura/>
             nyagrodhādirgaṇo yas tu kākolyādiś ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.79"> tau pittaduṣṭe dātavyau kaṣāyādiṣu saptasu |
            <caesura/>
             āragvadhādis tu gaṇo yaś coṣṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.80"> tau deyau kaphaduṣṭe tu saṃsṛṣṭe saṃyatā gaṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātātmakānugararujān sāsrāvānapi ca vraṇān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.81"> sakṣaumayavasarpirbhir dhūpanāṅgaiś ca dhūpayet |
            <caesura/>
             pariśuṣkālpamāṃsānāṃ gambhīrāṇāṃ tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.82"> kuryād utsādanīyāni sarpīṃṣyālepanāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsāśināṃ ca māṃsāni bhakṣayed vidhivan naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.83"> viśuddhamanasas tasya māṃsaṃ māṃsena vardhate |
            <caesura/>
             utsannamṛdumāṃsānāṃ vraṇānāmavasādanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.84"> kuryād dravyair yathoddiṣṭaiś cūrṇitair madhunā saha |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭhinānām amāṃsānāṃ duṣṭānāṃ matiriśvanā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.85"> mṛdvī kriyā vidhātavyā śoṇitaṃ cāpi mokṣayet |
            <caesura/>
             vātaghnauṣadhasaṃyuktān snehān sekāṃś ca pūrayet |
            <caesura/>
             kāsīsaṃ rocanāṃ tutthaṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.86"> mṛdutvamāśurohaṃ ca gāḍho bandhaḥ karoti hi| varṇeṣu
            mṛdumāṃseṣu dāruṇīkaraṇaṃ hitam| dhavapriyaṅgvaśokānāṃ rohiṇyāś ca
            tvacastathā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.87"> triphalādhātakīpuṣparodhrasarjarasān samān| kṛtvā
            sūkṣmāṇi cūrṇāni vraṇaṃ tairavacūrṇayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.88"> utsannamāṃsān kaṭhinān kaṇḍūyuktāṃścirotthitān| tathaiva
            khalu duḥśodhyāñ śodhayet kṣārakarmaṇā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.89"> sravato 'śmabhavānmūtraṃ ye cānye raktavāhinaḥ|
            niḥśeṣacchinnasandhīṃś ca sādhayed agnikarmaṇā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.90"> durūḍhatvāt tu śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇakarma hitaṃ bhavet|
            bhallātakān vāsayet tu kṣīre prāṅmūtrabhāvitān| tato dvidhā cchedayitvā lauhe
            kumbhe nidhāpayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.91"> kumbhe+anyasmin nikhāte tu taṃ kumbhamatha yojayet|
            mukhaṃ mukhena sandhāya gomayairdāhayettataḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.92"> yaḥ snehaścyavate tasmād grāhayettaṃ śanairbhiṣak|
            grāmyānūpaśaphān dagdhvā sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.93"> tailenānena saṃsṛṣṭaṃ śuklam ālepayed vraṇam|
            bhallātakavidhānena sārasnehāṃs tu kārayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.94"> ye ca kecit phalasnehā vidhānaṃ teṣu pūrvavat|
            durūḍhatvāt tu kṛṣṇānāṃ pāṇḍukarma hitaṃ bhavet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.95"> saptarātraṃ sthitaṃ kṣīre chāgale rohiṇīphalam| tenaiva
            piṣṭaṃ suślakṣṇaṃ savarṇakaraṇaṃ hitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.96"> navaṃ kapālikācūrṇaṃ vaidulaṃ sarjanāma ca| kāsīsaṃ
            madhukaṃ caiva kṣaudrayuktaṃ pralepayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.97"> kapitthimuddhṛte māṃse mūtreṇājena pūrayet| kāsīsaṃ
            rocanāṃ tutthaṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.98"> veṇunirlekhanaṃ cāpi prapunnāḍarasāñjanam |
            <caesura/>
             adhastādarjunasyaitanmāsaṃ bhūmau nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.99"> māsādūrdhvaṃ tatas tena kṛṣṇam ālepayed vraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             kukkuṭāṇḍakapālāni katakaṃ madhukaṃ samam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.100"> tathā samudramaṇḍūkī maṇicūrṇaṃ ca dāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             guṭikā mūtrapiṣṭāstā vraṇānāṃ pratisāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.101"> hastidantamasīṃ kṛtvā mukhyaṃ caiva rasāñjanam |
            <caesura/>
             romāṇyetena jāyante lepātpāṇitaleṣv api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.102"> catuṣpadānāṃ tvagromakhuraśṛṅgāsthibhasmanā |
            <caesura/>
             tailāktā cūrṇitā bhūmir bhaved romavatī punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.103"> kāsīsaṃ naktamālasya pallavāṃś caiva saṃharet |
            <caesura/>
             kapittharasapiṣṭāni romasañjananaṃ param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.104"> romākīrṇo vraṇo yas tu na samyaguparohati |
            <caesura/>
             kṣurakartarisandaṃśaus tasya romāṇi nirharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.105"> śaṅkhacūrṇasya bhāgau dvau haritālaṃ ca bhāgikam |
            <caesura/>
             śuktena saha piṣṭāni lomaśātanam uttamam ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.106"> tailaṃ bhallātakasyātha snuhīkṣīraṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             pragṛhyaikatra matimān romaśātanam uttamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.107"> kadalīdīrghavṛntābhyāṃ bhasmālaṃ lavaṇaṃ śamībījaṃ
            śītodapiṣṭaṃ vā romaśātanamācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.108"> āgāragodhikāpucchaṃ rambhā ''ālaṃ bījamaiṅgudam |
            <caesura/>
             dagdhvā tadbhasmatailāmbu sūryapakvaṃ kacāntakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.109"> vātaduṣṭo vraṇo yas tu rūkṣaś cātyarthavedanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             adhaḥkāye viśeṣeṇa tatra bastir vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.110"> mūtrāghāte mūtradoṣe śukradoṣe+aśmarīvraṇe |
            <caesura/>
             tathaivārtavadoṣe ca bastir apy uttaro hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.111"> yasmācchudhyati bandhena vraṇo yāti ca mārdavam |
            <caesura/>
             rohaty api ca niḥśaṅkas tasmād bandho vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.112"> sthirāṇāmalpamāṃsānāṃ raukṣyādanuparohatām |
            <caesura/>
             patradānaṃ bhavet kāryaṃ yathādoṣaṃ yathartu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.113"> eraṇḍabhūrjapūtīkaharidrāṇāṃ tu vātaje |
            <caesura/>
             patramāśvabalaṃ yac ca kāśmarīpatram eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.114"> patrāṇi kṣīravṛkṣāṇāmaudakāni tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             dūṣite raktapittābhyāṃ vraṇe dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.115"> pāṭhāmūrvāguḍūcīnāṃ kākamācīharidrayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             patraṃ ca śukanāsāyā yojayet kaphaje vraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.116"> akarkaśamavicchinnamajīrṇaṃ sukumārakam |
            <caesura/>
             ajantujagdhaṃ mṛdu ca patraṃ guṇavaducyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.117"> snehamauṣadhasāraṃ ca paṭṭaḥ patrāntarīkṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gādatte yattataḥ patraṃ lepasyopari dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.118"> śaityauṣṇyajananārthāya snehasaṃgrahaṇāya ca |
            <caesura/>
             dattauṣadheṣu dātavyaṃ patraṃ vaidyena jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.119"> makṣikā vraṇamāgatya niḥkṣipanti yadā kṛmīn |
            <caesura/>
             śvayathurbhakṣite tais tu jāyate bhṛśadāruṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.120"> tīvrā rujo vicitrāś ca raktāsrāvaś ca jāyate |
            <caesura/>
             surasādirhitas tatra dhāvane pūraṇe tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.121"> saptaparṇakarañjārkanimbarājādanatvacaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hitā gomūtrapiṣṭāś ca sekaḥ kṣārodakena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.122"> pracchādya māṃsapeśyā vā kṛmīn apahared vraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             viṃśatiṃ kṛmijātīs tu vaksyāmyupari bhāgaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.123"> dīrghakālāturāṇāṃ tu kṛśānāṃ vraṇaśoṣiṇām |
            <caesura/>
             bṛṃhaṇīyo vidhiḥ sarvaḥ kāyāgniṃ parirakṣatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.124"> viṣajuṣṭasya vijñānāṃ viṣaniścayam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             cikitsitaṃ ca vakṣyāmi kalpeṣu pratibhāgaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.125"> kaṇḍūmantaḥ saśophāś ca ye ca jatrūpari vraṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śirovirecanaṃ teṣu vidadhyātkuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.126"> rujāvanto 'nilāviṣṭā rūkṣā ye cordhvajatrujāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇeṣu teṣu kartavyaṃ nasyaṃ vaidyena jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.127"> doṣapracyāvanārthāya rujādāhakṣayāya ca |
            <caesura/>
             jihvādantasamutthasya haraṇārthaṃ malasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.128"> śodhano ropaṇaś caiva vraṇasya mukhajasya vai |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇo vā yadi vā śītaḥ kavalagraha iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.129"> ūrdhvajatrugatān rogān vraṇāṃś ca kaphavātajān |
            <caesura/>
             śophasrāvarujāyuktān dhūmapānair upācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.130"> kṣatoṣmaṇo nigrahārthaṃ sandhānārthaṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             sadyovraṇeṣvāyateṣu kṣaudrasarpir vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.131"> avagāḍhāstvaṇumukhā ye vraṇāḥ śalyapīḍitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nivṛttahastoddharaṇā yantraṃ teṣu vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.132"> laghumātro laghuś caiva snigdha uṣṇo 'gnidīpanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvavraṇibhyo deyas tu sadā ''āhāro vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.133"> niśācarebhyo rakṣyas tu nityam eva kṣatāturaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rakṣāvidhānair uddiṣṭair yamaiḥ saniyamais tatahā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.134"> ṣaṇmūlo 'ṣṭaparigrāhī pañcalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaṣṭyā cidhānair nirdiṣṭaiś caturbhiḥ sādhyate vraṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.135"> yo 'lpauṣadhakṛto yogo bahugranthabhayānmayā |
            <caesura/>
             dravyāṇāṃ tatsamānānāṃ tatrāvāpo na duṣyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.136"> prasaṅgābhihito yo vā bahudurlabhabheṣajaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathopapatti tatrāpi kāryam eva cikitsitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.137"> goṇoktam api yaddravyaṃ bhaved vyādhāvayaugikam |
            <caesura/>
             tad uddhared yaugikaṃ tu prakṣiped apy akīrtitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.138"> upadravās tu vividhā vraṇasya vraṇitasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             tatra gandhādayaḥ pañca vraṇasyopadravāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.139"> jvarātisārau mūrcchā ca hikkā cchardirarocakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śvāsakāsāvipākāś ca tṛṣṇā ca vraṇitasya tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.140"> vraṇakriyāsvevamāsu vyāsenoktāsv apikriyām |
            <caesura/>
             bhūyo 'pyupari vakṣyāmi sadyovraṇacikitsite ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne dvivraṇīyacikitsitaṃ nāma
            prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||1 ||</p>
        </div>



        <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

          <head>dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.1"> athātaḥ sadyovraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.3"> dhanvantarir dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭho vāgviśāradaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viśvāmitrasutaṃ śiṣyam ṛṣiṃ suśrutam anvaśāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.4"> nānādhārāmukhaiḥ śastrair nānāsthānanipātitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nānārūpā vraṇā ye syus teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.5"> āyatāś caturasrāś ca tryasrā maṇḍalinas tathā |
            <caesura/>
             ardhacandrapratīkāśā viśālāḥ kuṭilās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.6"> śarāvanimnamadhyāś ca yavamadhyās tathā 'pare |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃprakārākṛtayo bhavanty āgantavo vraṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.7"> doṣajā vā svayaṃ bhinnā na tu vaidyanimittajāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhiṣagvraṇākṛtijño hi na moham adhigacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.8"> bhṛśaṃ durdarśarūpeṣu vraṇeṣu vikṛteṣv api |
            <caesura/>
             anantākṛtir āgantuḥ sa bhiṣagbhiḥ purātanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.9"> samāsato lakṣaṇataḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             chinnaṃ bhinnaṃ tathā viddhaṃ kṣataṃ piccitam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.10"> ghṛṣṭam āhus tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             tiraścīna ṛjurvā 'pi yo vraṇaś cāyato bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.11"> gātrasya pātanaṃ cāpi chinnam ity upadiśyate |
            <caesura/>
             kuntaśaktyṛṣṭikhaṅgāgraviṣāṇādibhir āśayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.12"> hataḥ kiñcit sravet tad dhi bhinnalakṣaṇam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             sthānāny āmāgnipakvānāṃ mūtrasya rudhirasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.13"> hṛduṇḍukaḥ phupphusaś ca koṣṭha ity abhidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             tasmin bhinne raktapūrṇe jvaro dāhaś ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.14"> mūtramārgagudāsyebhyo raktaṃ ghrāṇāc ca gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchāśvāsatṛḍādhmānamabhaktacchanda eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.15"> viṇmūtravātasaṅgaś ca svedāsrāvo 'kṣiraktatā |
            <caesura/>
             lohagandhitvam āsyasya gātradaurgandhyam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.16"> hṛcchūlaṃ pārśvayoś cāpi viśeṣaṃ cātra me śṛṇu |
            <caesura/>
             āmāśayasthe rudhire rudhiraṃ saṃgṛhya samutthāpya mahābalāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhavaty antaḥpraveśas tu yathā nirdhunuyus tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.17"> ādhmānamatimātraṃ ca śūlaṃ ca bhṛśadāruṇam| pakvāśayagate
            cāpi rujo gauravam eva ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.18"> śītatā cāpy adho nāmeḥ khebhyo raktasya cāgamaḥ|
            abhinne+apyāśaye+antrāṇāṃ khaiḥ sūkṣmairantrapūraṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.19"> pihitāsye ghaṭe yadvallakṣyate tasya gauravam|
            sūkṣmāsyaśalyābhihataṃ yadaṅgaṃ tvāśayādvinā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.20"> uttuṇḍitaṃ nirgataṃ vā tadviddham iti nirdiśet|
            nāticchinnaṃ nātibhinnamubhayor lakṣaṇānvitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.21"> viṣamaṃ vraṇamaṅge yattat kṣataṃ tvabhinirdiśet|
            prahārapīḍanābhyāṃ tu yadaṅgaṃ pṛthutāṃ gatam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.22"> sāsthi tat piccitaṃ vidyānmajjaraktapariplutam|
            vigatatvagyadaṅgaṃ hi saṃgharṣādanyathā+api vā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.23"> uṣāsrāvānvitaṃ tattu ghṛṣṭamity upadiśyate| chinne bhinne
            tathā viddhe kṣate vā+asṛgatisravet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.24"> raktakṣayādrujas tatra karoti pavano bhṛśam| snehapānaṃ
            hitaṃ tatra tatseko vihitastathā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.25"> veśavāraiḥ sakṛśaraiḥ susnigdhaiścopanāhanam|
            dhānyasvedāṃś ca kurvīta snigdhānyālepanāni ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.26"> vātaghnauṣadhasiddhaiśca snehairbastirvidhīyate| piccite
            ca vighṛṣṭe ca nātisravapi śoṇitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.27"> agacchati bhṛśaṃ tasmin dāhaḥ pākaś ca jāyate| tatroṣmaṇo
            nigrahārthaṃ tathā dāhaprapākayoḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.28"> śītam ālepanaṃ kāryaṃ pariṣekaśca śītalaḥ| ṣaṭsveteṣu
            yathokteṣu chinnādiṣu samāsataḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.29"> jñeyaṃ samarpitaṃ sarvaṃ sadyovraṇacikitsitam| ata
            ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi chinnānāṃ tu cikitsitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.30"> ye vraṇā vivṛtāḥ kecicchiraḥpārśvāvalambinaḥ| tān sīvyed
            vidhinoktena badhnīyād gāḍham eva ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.31"> karṇaṃ sthānādapahṛtaṃ sthāpayitvā yathāsthitam| sīvyed
            yathoktaṃ tailena srotaś cābhipratarpayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.32"> kṛkāṭikānte chinne tu gacchatyapi samīraṇe| samyaṅniveśya
            badhnīyāt sīvyec cāpi nirantaram|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.33"> ājena sapiṣā caivaṃ pariṣekaṃ tu kārayet| uttāno 'nnaṃ
            samaśnīyācchayīta ca suyantritaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.34"> śākhāsu patitāṃstiryak prahārān vivṛtān bhṛśam| sīvyet
            samyaṅniveśyāśu sandhyasthīnyanupūrvaśaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.35"> baddhvā vellitakenāśu tatastailena secayet| carmaṇā
            gophaṇābandhaḥ kāryo yo vā hito bhavet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.36"> pṛṣṭhe vraṇo yasya bhaved uttānaṃ śāyayet tu tam| ato
            'nyathā corasije śāyayet puruṣaṃ vraṇe|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.37"> chinnāṃ niḥśeṣataḥ śākhāṃ dagdhvā tailena buddhimān|
            badhnīyāt kośabandhena prāptaṃ kāryaṃ ca ropaṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.38"> candanaṃ padmakaṃ rodhramutpalāni priyaṅgavaḥ| haridrā
            madhukaṃ caiva payaḥ syādatra cāṣṭamam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.39"> tailamebhir vipakvaṃ tu pradhānaṃ vraṇaropaṇam| candanaṃ
            karkaṭākhyā ca sahe māṃsyāhvayā+amṛtā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.40"> hareṇavo mṛṇālaṃ ca triphalā padmakotpale| trayodaśāṅgaṃ
            trivṛtametadvā payasā+anvitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.41"> tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sekārthe hitaṃ tu vraṇaropaṇe| ata
            ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhinnānāṃ tu cikitsitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.42"> bhinnaṃ netramakarmaṇyamabhinnaṃ lambate tu yat|
            tanniveśya yathāsthānamavyāviddhasiraṃ śanaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.43"> pīḍayet pāṇinā samyak padmapattrāntareṇa tu| tato 'sya
            tarpaṇaṃ kāryaṃ nasyaṃ cānena sarpiṣā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.44"> ājaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣīrapātraṃ madhukaṃ cotpalāni ca|
            jīvakarṣabhakau caiva piṣṭvā sarpir vipācayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.45"> sarvanetrābhighāte tu sarpiretat praśasyate| udarānmedaso
            vartirnirgatā yasya dehinaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.46"> kaṣāyabhasmamṛtkīrṇāṃ baddhvā sūtreṇa sūtravit|
            agnitaptena śastreṇa chindyānmadhusamāyutam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.47"> baddhvā vraṇaṃ sujīrṇe+anne sarpiṣaḥ pānamiṣyate|
            snehapānādṛte cāpi payaḥpānaṃ vidhīyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.48"> śarkarāmadhuyaṣṭibhyāṃ lākṣayā vā śvadaṃṣṭrayā|
            citrāsamanvitaṃ caiva rujādāhavināśanam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.49"> āṭopo maraṇaṃ vā syācchūlo vā+acchidyamānayā|
            medogranthau tu yattailaṃ vakṣyate tac ca yojayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.50"> tvaco 'tītya sirādīni bhittvā vā parihṛtya vā| koṣṭhe
            pratiṣṭhitaṃ śalyaṃ kuryād uktānupadravān|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.51"> tatrāntarlohitaṃ pāṇḍuṃ śītapādakarānanam| śītocchvāsaṃ
            raktanetramānaddhaṃ ca vivarjayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.52"> āmāśayasthe rudhire vamanaṃ pathyamucyate| pakvāśayasthe
            deyaṃ ca virecanamasaṃśayam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.53"> āsthāpanaṃ ca niḥshehaṃ kāryamuṣṇair viśodhanaiḥ|
            yavakolakulatthānāṃ niḥsnehena rasena ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.54"> bhuñjītānnaṃ yavāgūṃ vā pibet saindhavasaṃyutām|
            atiniḥsrutarakto vā bhinnakoṣṭhaḥ pibed asṛk|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.55"> svamārgapratipannās tu yasya viṇmūtramārutāḥ| vyupadravaḥ
            sa bhinne+api koṣṭhe jīvati mānavaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.56"> abhinnamantraṃ niṣkrāntaṃ praveśyaṃ nānyathā bhavet|
            pipīlikāśirograstaṃ tadapyeke vadanti tu|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.57"> prakṣālya payasā digdhaṃ tṛṇśoṇitapāṃśubhiḥ| praveśayet
            kṛttanakho ghṛtenāktaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.58"> praveśayet kṣīrasiktaṃ śuṣkamatraṃ ghṛtāplutam|
            aṅgulyā+abhimṛśet kaṇṭhaṃ jalenodvejayed api|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.59"> hastapādeṣu saṃgṛhya samutthāpya mahābalāḥ| bhavaty
            antaḥpraveśas tu yathā nirdhunuyustathā|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.60"> tathā 'ntrāṇi viśantyantaḥ svāṃ kalāṃ pīḍayanti ca |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇālpatvād bahutvād vā duṣpraveśaṃ bhavet tu yat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.61"> tadāpāṭhya pramāṇena bhiṣagantraṃ parveśayet |
            <caesura/>
             yathāsthānaṃ niveṣṭe ca vraṇaṃ sīvyed atandriyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.62"> sthānādapetamādatte prāṇān gupitam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             veṣṭayitvā tu paṭṭena ghṛtasekaṃ pradāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.63"> ghṛtaṃ pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ ca citrātailasamanvitam |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdukriyārthaṃ śakṛto vāyoś cādhaḥpravṛttaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.64"> tatastailamidaṃ kuryād ropaṇārthaṃ cikitsakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tvaco 'śvakarṇadhavayor mocakīmeṣaśṛṅgayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.65"> śallakyarjunayoś cāpi vidāryāḥ kṣīriṇāṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             balāmūlāni cāhṛtya tailametair vipācayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.66"> vraṇaṃ saṃropayet tena varṣamātraṃ yateta ca |
            <caesura/>
             pādau nirastamuṣkasya jalena prokṣya cākṣiṇī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.67"> praveśya tunnasevanyā muṣkau sīvyet tataḥ param |
            <caesura/>
             kāryo gophaṇikābandhaḥ kaṭyām āveśya yantrakam || </l>



          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.68"> na kuryāt snehasekaṃ ca tena klidyati hi vraṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
            <caesura/>
             kālānusāryāgurvelājātīcandanapadmakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.69"> śilādārvyamṛtātutthaistailaṃ kurvīta ropaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             śiraso 'apahṛte śalye bālavartiṃ niveśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.70"> bālavartyām adattāyāṃ mastuluṅgaṃ vraṇāt sravet |
            <caesura/>
             hanyād enaṃ tato vāyus tasmād evam upācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.71"> vraṇe rohati caikaikaṃ śanairbālamapakṣipet |
            <caesura/>
             gātrādapahṛte 'nyasmāt snehavartiṃ praveśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.72"> kṛte niḥśoṇite cāpi vidhiḥ sadyaḥkṣate hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dūrābagāḍhāḥ sūkṣmāḥ syurye vraṇāstān viśoṇitān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.73"> kṛtvā sūkṣmeṇa netreṇa cakratailena tarpayet |
            <caesura/>
             samaṅgāṃ rajanīṃ padmāṃ trivargaṃ tutthameva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.74"> viḍaṅgaṃ kaṭukāṃ pathyāṃ guḍūcīṃ sakarañjikām |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛtya vipacet kāle tailaṃ ropaṇamuttamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.75"> tālīśaṃ padmakaṃ māṃsī hareṇvagurucandanam |
            <caesura/>
             haridre padmabījāni sośīraṃ madhukaṃ ca taiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.76"> pakvaṃ sadyovraṇeṣūktaṃ tailaṃ ropaṇamuttamam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣate kṣatavidhiḥ kāryaḥ piccite bhagnavadvidhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.77"> ghṛṣṭe rujo nigṛhyāśu cūrṇair upacared vraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             viśliṣṭadehaṃ patitaṃ mathitaṃ hatam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.78"> vāsayettailapūrṇāyāṃ droṇyāṃ māṃsarasāśanam |
            <caesura/>
             ayameva vidhiḥ kāryaḥ kṣīṇe marmahate tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.79"> ropaṇe saparīṣeke pāne ca vraṇināṃ sadā |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā saṃyojyaṃ śarīrartūnavekṣya hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.80"> ghṛtāni yāni vakṣyāmi yatnataḥ pittavidradhau |
            <caesura/>
             sadyovraṇeṣu deyāni tāni vaidyena jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.81"> sadyaḥkṣatavraṇaṃ vaidyaḥ saśūlaṃ pariṣecayet |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiṣā nātiśītena balātailena vā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.82"> samaṅgāṃ rajanīṃ padmāṃ pathyāṃ tutthaṃ suvarcalām |
            <caesura/>
             padmakaṃ rodhramadhukaṃ viḍaṅgāni hareṇukām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.83"> tālīśapatraṃ naladaṃ candanaṃ padmakeśaram |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhośīralākṣāś ca kṣīriṇāṃ cāpi pallavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.84"> priyālabījaṃ tindukyāstaruṇāni phalāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             yathālābhaṃ samāhṛtya tailamebhir vipācayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.85"> sadyovraṇānāṃ sarveṣāmaduṣṭānāṃ tu ropaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyamadhurāḥ śītāḥ kriyāḥ snigdhāś ca yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.86"> sadyovraṇānāṃ saptāhaṃ paścāt pūrvoktamācaret |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭavraṇeṣu kartavyamūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.87"> viśoṣaṇaṃ tathā++āhāraḥ śoṇitasya ca mokṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyaṃ rājavṛkṣādau surasādau ca dhāvanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.88"> tayoreva kaṣāyeṇa tailaṃ śodhanamiṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             kṣārakalpena vā tailaṃ kṣāradravyeṣu sādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.89"> dravantī cirabilvaś ca dantī citrakameva ca |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthvīkā nimbapatrāṇi kāsīsaṃ tutthameva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.90"> trivṛttejovatī nīlī haridre saindhavaṃ tilāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhūmikadambaḥ suvahā śukākhyā lāṅgalāhvayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.91"> naipālī jālinī caiva madayantī mṛgādanī |
            <caesura/>
             sudhāmūrvārkakīṭāriharitālakarañjikāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.92"> yathopapatti kartavyaṃ tailam etais tu śodhanam |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaṃ vā yadi vā prāptaṃ kalkāḥ saṃśodhanāstathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.93"> saindhavatrivṛderaṇḍapatrakalkastu vātike |
            <caesura/>
             trivṛddharidrāmadhukakalkaḥ paitte tilairyutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.94"> kaphaje tilatejohvādantīsvarjikacitrakāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭavraṇavidhiḥ kāryo mehakuṣṭhavraṇeṣvapi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.95"> ṣaḍvidhaḥ prāk pradiṣṭo yaḥ sadyovraṇaviniścayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nātaḥ śakyaṃ paraṃ vaktumapi niścitavādibhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.96"> upasargair nipātaiś ca tat tu paṇḍitamāninaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kecit saṃyojya bhāṣante bahudhā mānagarvitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.2.97"> bahu tadbhāṣitaṃ teṣāṃ ṣaṭsveṣvevāvatiṣṭhate |
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣā iva sāmānye ṣaṭtvaṃ tu paramaṃ matam||</l>
          <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sadyocraṇacikitsitaṃ nāma dvitīyo
            'adhyāyaḥ ||2||</trailer>
        </div>


        <div n="3" subtype="adhyāya">
          <head>tṛtīyo 'adhyāyaḥ|</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.1"> athāto bhagnānāṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.3"> alpāśino 'anātmavato jantorvātātmakasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             upadravair vā juṣṭasya bhagnaṃ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.4"> lavaṇaṃ kaṭukaṃ kṣāramamlaṃ maithunamātapam |
            <caesura/>
             vyāyāmaṃ ca na seveta bhagno rūkṣānnameva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.5"> śālirmāṃsarasaḥ kṣīraṃ sarpiryūṣaḥ satīnajaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bṛṃhaṇaṃ cānnapānaṃ syāddeyaṃ bhagnāya jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.6"> madhūkodumbarāśvatthapalāśakakubhatvacaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vaṃśasarjavaṭānāṃ ca kuśārthamupasaṃharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.7"> ālepanārthaṃ mañjiṣṭhāṃ madhukaṃ raktacandanam |
            <caesura/>
             śatadhautaghṛtonmiśraṃ śālipiṣṭaṃ ca saṃharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.8"> saptāhād atha saptāhāt saumyeṣv ṛtuṣu bandhanam |
            <caesura/>
             sādhāraṇeṣu kartavyaṃ pañcame pañcame 'hani || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.9"> āgneyeṣu tryahā tu kuryād bhagnadoṣavaśena vā |
            <caesura/>
             tatrātiśithilaṃ baddhe sandhisthairyaṃ na jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.10"> gāḍhenāpi tvagādīnāṃ śopho ruk pāka eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt sādhāraṇaṃ bandhaṃ bhagne śaṃsanti tadvidaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.11"> nyagrodhādikaṣāyaṃ tu suśītaṃ pariṣecane |
            <caesura/>
             pañcamūlīvipakvaṃ tu kṣīraṃ kuryāt savedane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.12"> sukhoṣṇam avacāryaṃ vā cakratailaṃ vijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             vibhajya kālaṃ doṣaṃ ca doṣaghnauṣadhasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.13"> pariṣekaṃ pradehaṃ ca vidadhyāc chītam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             gṛṣṭikṣīraṃ sasarpiṣkaṃ madhurauṣadhasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.14"> śītalaṃ lākṣayā yuktaṃ prātarbhagnaḥ pibennaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             savraṇasya tu bhagnasya vraṇaṃ sarpirmadhūttaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.15"> pratisārya kaṣāyaistu śeṣaṃ bhagnavadācaret |
            <caesura/>
             prathame vayasi tvevaṃ bhagnaṃ sukaramādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.16"> alpadoṣasya jantostu kāle ca śiśirātmake |
            <caesura/>
             prathame vayasi tvevaṃ māsāt sandhiḥ sthiro bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.17"> madhyame dviguṇāt kālāduttare triguṇāt smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             avanāmitam unnahyed unnataṃ cavapīḍayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.18"> āñched atikṣiptam adho gataṃ copari vartayet |
            <caesura/>
             āñchanaiḥ pīḍanaiś caiva saṅkṣepair bandhanais tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.19"> sandhīñcharīre sarvāṃstu calānapyacalānapi |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.20"> utpiṣṭam atha viśliṣṭaṃ sandhiṃ vaidyo na ghaṭṭayet |

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.3.70"> bhagnaṃ sandhimanāviddhamahīnāṅgamanulbaṇam |
