          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.10"> gomūtragandhi yac cāpi tat pradhānaṃ pracakṣate |
            <caesura/>
             tadbhāvitaṃ sāragaṇair hṛtadoṣo dinodaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.11"> pibet sārodakenaiva ślakṣṇapiṣṭaṃ yathābalam |
            <caesura/>
             jāṅgalena rasenānnaṃ tasmiñjīrṇe tu bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.12"> upayujya tulāmevaṃ girijādamṛtopamāt |
            <caesura/>
             vapurvarṇabalopeto madhumehavivarjitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.13"> jīved varṣaśataṃ pūrṇamajaro 'marasannibhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śataṃ śataṃ tulāyāṃ tu sahasraṃ daśataulike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.14"> bhallātakavidhānena parihāravidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mehaṃ kuṣṭhamapasmāramunmādaṃ ślīpadaṃ garam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.15"> śoṣaṃ śophārśasī gulmaṃ pāṇḍutāṃ viṣamajvaram |
            <caesura/>
             apohatyacirātkālācchilājatu niṣevitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.16"> na so 'sti rogo yaṃ cāpi nihanyānna śilājatu |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāṃ cirasaṃbhūtāṃ bhinatti ca tathā 'śmarīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.17"> bhāvanāloḍane cāsya kartavye bheṣajair hitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃ ca mākṣikaṃ dhātuṃ tāpījamamṛtopamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.18"> madhuraṃ kāñcanābhāsamamlaṃ vā rajataprabham |
            <caesura/>
             piban hanti jarākuṣṭhamehapāṇḍvāmayakṣayān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.19"> tadbhāvitaḥ kapotāṃś ca kulatthāṃś ca vivarjayet |
            <caesura/>
             pañcakarmaguṇātītaṃ śraddhāvantaṃ jijīviṣum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.20"> yogenānena matimān sādhayed api kuṣṭhanam |
            <caesura/>
             vṛkṣās tuvarakā ye syuḥ paścimārṇava<pc> </pc>bhūmiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.21"> vīcītaraṅgavikṣepamārutoddhūtapallavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             teṣāṃ phalāni gṛhṇīyāt supakvānyambudāgame || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.22"> majjāṃ tebhyo 'pi saṃhṛtya śoṣayitvā vicūrṇya ca |
            <caesura/>
             tilavat pīḍayed droṇyāṃ srāvayed vā kusumbhavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.23"> tattailaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ pacedātoyasaṃkṣayāt |
            <caesura/>
             avatārya karīṣe ca pakṣamātraṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.24"> snigdhaḥ svinno hṛtamalaḥ pakṣādūrdhvaṃ prayatnavān |
            <caesura/>
             caturthabhaktāntaritaḥ śuklādau divase śubhe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.25"> mantrapūtasya tailasya pibenmātrāṃ yathābalam |
            <caesura/>
             tatra mantraṃ pravakṣyāmi yenedam abhimantryate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.26"> majjasāra mahāvīrya sarvān dhātūn viśodhaya |
            <caesura/>
             śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇistvāmājñāpayate 'cyutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.27"> tenāsyor dhvamadhaś cāpi doṣā yāntyasakṛttataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             asnehalavaṇāṃ sāyaṃ yavāgūṃ śītalāṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.28"> pañcāhaṃ prapibettailamanena vidhinā naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pakṣaṃ pariharec cāpi mudgayūṣaudanāśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.29"> pañcabhir divasair evaṃ sarvakuṣṭhair vimucyate |
            <caesura/>
             tad eva khadirakvāthe triguṇe sādhu sādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.30"> nihitaṃ pūrvavat pakṣāt pibenmāsamatandritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tenābhyaktaśarīraś ca kurvītāhāramīritam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.31"> bhinnasvaraṃ raktanetraṃ viśīrṇaṃ kṛmibhakṣitam |
            <caesura/>
             anenāśu prayogeṇa sādhayet kuṣṭhinaṃ naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.32"> sarpirmadhuyutaṃ pītaṃ tad eva khadirāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             pakṣimāṃsarasāhāraṃ karoti dviśatāyuṣam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.33"> tad eva nasye pañcāśaddivasānupayojitam |
            <caesura/>
             vapuṣmantaṃ śrutidharaṃ karoti triśatāyuṣam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.34"> śodhayanti naraṃ pītā majjānas tasya mātrayā |
            <caesura/>
             mahāvīryastuvarakaḥ kuṣṭhamehāpahaḥ paraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.13.35"> sāntardhūmas tasya majjā tu dagdhaḥ kṣiptastaile
            saindhavaṃ cāñjanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             paillyaṃ hanyādarmanaktāndhyakācān nīlīrogaṃ taimiraṃ cāñjanena ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne madhumehacikitsitaṃ nāma
            trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||13 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
          <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.1"> athāta udarāṇāṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.3"> aṣṭāv udarāṇi pūrvam uddiṣṭāni |
            <caesura/>
             teṣv asādhyaṃ baddhagudaṃ parisrāvi ca; avaśiṣṭāni kṛcchrasādhyāni; sarvāṇy
            eva pratyākhyāyopakrameta | teṣv ādyaś caturvargo bheṣajasādhyaḥ, uttaraḥ
            śastrasādhyaḥ, kālaprakarṣāt sarvāṇyeva śastrasādhyāni varjayitavyāni vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.4"> udarī tu
            gurvabhiṣyandirūkṣavidāhisnigdhapiśitapariṣekāvagāhān pariharet;
            śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmanīvārān nityam aśnīyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.5"> tatra vātodariṇaṃ vidārigandhādisiddhena sarpiṣā
            snehayitvā, tilvakavipakvenānulomya, citrāphalatailapragāḍhena
            vidārigandādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayec ca, sālvaṇena copanāhayed udaraṃ,
            bhojayec cainaṃ vidārigandhādisiddhena kṣīreṇa jāṅgalarasena ca, svedayec
            cābhīkṣṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.6"> pittodariṇaṃ tu madhuragaṇavipakvena sarpiṣā snehayitvā,
            śyāmātriphalātrivṛdvipakvenānulomya, śarkarāmadhughṛtapragāḍhena
            nyagrodhādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayec ca, pāyasenopanāhayed udaraṃ, bhojayec
            cainaṃ vidārigandhādisiddhena payasā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.7"> śleṣmodariṇaṃ tu pippalyādikaṣāyasiddhena
            sarpiṣopasnehya, snuhīkṣīravipakvenānulomya,
            trikaṭukamūtrakṣāratailapragāḍhena muṣkakādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayec ca,
            śaṇātasīdhātakīkiṇvasarṣapamūlakabījakalkaiś copanāhayed udaraṃ, bhojayec
            cainaṃ trikaṭukapragāḍhena kulatthayūṣeṇa pāyasena vā, svedayec cābhīkṣṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.8"> dūṣyodariṇaṃ tu pratyākhyāya
            saptalāśaṅkhinīsvarasasiddhena sarpiṣā viracayen māsam ardhamāsaṃ vā,
            mahāvṛkṣakṣīrasurāgomūtrasiddhena vā; śuddhakoṣṭhaṃ tu
            madyenāśvamārakaguñjākākādanīmūlakalkaṃ pāyayet; ikṣukāṇḍāni vā kṛṣṇasarpeṇa
            daṃśayitvā bhakṣayed vallīphalāni vā, mūlajaṃ kandajaṃ vā viṣamā sevayet,
            tenāgado bhavaty anyaṃ vā bhāvam āpadyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.9"> bhavati cātra kupitānilamūlatvāt saṃcitatvān malasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             sarvodareṣu śaṃsanti bahuśas tv anulomanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.10"> ata ūrdhvaṃ sāmānyayogān vakṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā
            eraṇḍatailam aharahar māsaṃ dvau vā kevalaṃ mūtrayuktaṃ kṣīrayuktaṃ vā
            sevetodakavarjī, māhiṣaṃ vā mūtraṃ kṣīreṇa nirāhāraḥ saptarātram,
            uṣṭrīkṣīrāhāro vā 'nnavārivarjī pakṣaṃ, pippalīṃ vā māsaṃ pūrvoktena
            vidhānenāseveta, saindhavājamodāyuktaṃ vā nikumbhatailam,
            ārdraśṛṅgaverarasapātraśatasiddhaṃ vā vātaśūle 'vacāryaṃ,
            śṛṅgaverarasavipakvaṃ kṣīram āseveta, cavyaśṛṅgaverakalkaṃ vā payasā
            saraladevadārucitrakam eva vā, muraṅgīśālaparṇīśyāmāpunarnavākalkaṃ vā,
            jyotiṣkaphalatailaṃ vā kṣīreṇa svarjikāhiṅgumiśraṃ pibet, <ref
              rend="superscript                 footnote marker">*</ref>guḍadvitīyāṃ vā
            harītakīṃ bhakṣayet, srutīkṣīrabhāvitānāṃ vā pippalīnāṃ sahasraṃ kālena,
            pathyākṛṣṇācūrṇaṃ vā snuhīkṣīrabhāvitamutkārikāṃ pakvāṃ dāpayet;
            harītakīcūrṇaṃ prasthamāḍhake ghṛtasyāvāpyāṅgāreṣv abhivilāpya
            khajenābhimathyānuguptaṃ kṛtvā 'rdhamāsaṃ yavapalle vāsayet, tataś coddhṛtya
            parisrāvya harītakīkvāthāmladadhīnyāvāpya vipacet, tad yathā yogaṃ māsam
            ardhamāsaṃ vā pāyayet; gavye payasi mahāvṛkṣakṣīramāvāpya vipacet, vipakvaṃ
            cāvatārya śītībhūtaṃ manthānenābhimathya navanītamādāya bhūyo
            mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇaiva vipacet, tad yathā yogaṃ māsaṃ māsārdhaṃ vā pāyayet;
            cavyacitrakadantyativiṣākuṣṭhasārivātriphalājamodaharidrāśaṅkhinītrivṛttrikaṭukānām
            ardhakārṣikā bhāgā, rājavṛkṣaphalamajjñāmaṣṭau karṣāḥ, mahāvṛkṣakṣīrapale dve,
            gavāṃ kṣīramūtrayor aṣṭāvaṣṭau palāni, etat sarvaṃ ghṛtaprasthe samāvāpya
            vipacet, tad yathā yogaṃ māsam ardhamāsṃ vā pāyayet; etāni
            tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni sarpīṣy
            udaragulmavidradhyaṣṭhīlānāhakuṣṭhonmādāpasmāreṣūpayojyāni virecanārthaṃ;
            mūtrāsavāriṣṭasurāś cābhīkṣṇaṃ mahāvṛkṣakṣīrasaṃbhṛtāḥ seveta;
            virecanadravyakaṣāyaṃ vā śṛṅgaveradevadārupragāḍham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.11"> vamanavirecanaśirovirecanadravyāṇāṃ pālikābhāgāḥ
            pippalyādivacādiharidrādiparipaṭhitānāṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ ślakṣṇapiṣṭānāṃ
            yathoktānāṃ ca lavaṇānāṃ tat sarvaṃ mūtragaṇe prakṣipya mahāvṛkṣakṣīraprasthaṃ
            ca mṛdvagninā 'vaghaṭṭayan vipaced apradagdhakalkaṃ, tatsādhusiddham avatārya
            śītībhūtamakṣamātrā guṭikā vartayet, tāsām ekāṃ dve tisro vā guṭikā
            balāpekṣayā māsāṃs trīṃś caturo vā seveta, eṣā++<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>ānāhavartikriyā viśeṣeṇa
            mahāvyādhiṣūpayujyate (viśeṣeṇa) koṣṭhajāṃś ca kṛmīn apahanti
            kāsaśvāsakṛmikuṣṭhapratiśyāyārocakāvipākodāvartāṃś ca nāśayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.12">
            madanaphalamajjakuṭajajīmūtakekṣvākudhāmārgavatrivṛttrikaṭukasarṣapalavaṇāni
            mahāvṛkṣakṣīramūtrayor anyatareṇa piṣṭvā 'ṅguṣṭhamātrāṃ vartiṃ kṛtvodariṇa
            ānāhe tailalavaṇābhyaktagudasyaikāṃ dve tisro vā pāyau nidadhyāt, eṣā
            ''ānāhavartikriyā vātamūtrapurīṣodāvartādhmānānāheṣu vidheyā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.13"> plīhodariṇaḥ snigdhasvinnasya dadhnā bhuktavato
            vāmabāhau kūrparābhyantarataḥ sirāṃ vidhyet, vimardayec ca pāṇinā plīhānaṃ
            rudhirasyandanārthaṃ; tataḥ saṃśuddhadehaṃ samudraśuktikākṣāraṃ payasā
            pāyayeta, hiṅgusauvarcike vā kṣīreṇa, srutena palāśakṣāreṇa vā yavakṣāraṃ,
            kiṃśukakṣārodakena vā bahuśaḥ srutena yavakṣāraṃ,
            pārijātakekṣurakāpāmārgakṣāraṃ vā, tailasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ śobhāñjanakayūṣaṃ
            pippalīsaindhavacitrakayuktaṃ, pūtikarañjakṣāraṃ vā 'mlasrutaṃ
            viḍlavaṇapippalīprāgāḍham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.14">
            pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakaśṛṅgaverayavakṣārasaindhavānāṃ pālikā bhāgāḥ,
            ghṛtaprasthaṃ tattulyaṃ ca kṣīraṃ tadaikadhyaṃ vipācayet , etat ṣaṭpalakaṃ
            nāma sarpiḥ plīhāgnisaṅgagulmodarodāvartaśvayathupāṇḍurogakāsaśvāsapratiśyāyor
            dhvavātaviṣamajvarān apahanti | mandāgnirvā hiṅgvādikaṃ cūrṇam upayuñjīta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.15"> yakṛddālye 'py eṣa eva kriyāvibhāgaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣatas tu dakṣiṇabāhau sirāvyadhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.16"> maṇibandhaṃ sakṛnnāmya vāmāṅguṣṭhasamīritām |
            <caesura/>
             dahet sirāṃ śareṇāśu plīhno vaidyaḥ praśāntaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.17"> baddhagude parisrāviṇi ca snigdhasvinnasyābhyaktasyādho
            nābher vāmataś caturaṅgulam apahāya romarājyā udaraṃ pāṭayitvā
            caturaṅgulapramāṇamantrāṇi niṣkṛṣya nirīkṣya
            baddhagudasyāntrapratirodhakaramaśmānaṃ bālaṃ vā 'pohya malajātaṃ vā tato
            madhusarpirbhyām abhyajyāntrāṇi yathāsthānaṃ sthāpayitvā <ref
              rend="superscript               footnote marker">*</ref>bāhyaṃ vraṇam
            udarasya sīvyet | parisrāviṇy apy evam eva śalyamuddhṛtyāntrasrāvān
              saṃśodhya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>, tacchidramāntraṃ
            samādhāya kālapipīlikābhir daṃśayet, daṣṭe ca tāsāṃ kāyān apaharen na śirāṃsi,
            tataḥ pūrvavat sīvyet, saṃdhānaṃ ca yathoktaṃ kārayet, yaṣṭīmadhukamiśrayā ca
            kṛṣṇamṛdā 'valipya bandhenopacaret, tato nivātamāgāraṃ praveśyācārikam
            upadiśet, vāsayec cainaṃ tailadroṇyāṃ sarpirdroṇyāṃ vā payovṛttim iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.18"> dakodariṇas tu vātaharatailābhyaktasyoṣṇodakasvinnasya
            sthitasyāptaiḥ suparigṛhītasyākakṣāt pariveṣṭitasyādho nābher vāmataś
            caturaṅgulam apahāya romarājyā vrīhimukhenāṅguṣṭhodarapramāṇam avagāḍhaṃ
            vidhyet, tatra trapvādīnām anyatamasya nāḍīṃ dvidvārāṃ pakṣanāḍīṃ vā saṃyojya
            doṣodakam avasiñcet, toto nāḍīm apahṛtya tailalavaṇenābhyajya vraṇaṃ
            bandhenopacaret, na caikasminn eva divase sarvaṃ doṣodakam apaharet, sahasā hy
            apahṛte tṛṣṇājvarāṅgamardātīsāraśvāsakāsapādadāhā utpadyerann āpūryate vā
            bhṛśataram udaram asañjātaprāṇasya, tasmāt
            tṛtīyacaturthapañcamaṣaṣṭhāṣṭamadaśamadvādaśaṣoḍaśarātrāṇām anyatamam
            antarīkṛtya doṣodakam alpālpam avasiñcet; niḥsṛte ca doṣe gāḍhataram
            āvikakauśeyacarmaṇām anyatamena pariveṣṭayed udaraṃ, tathā nādhmāpayati vāyuḥ;
            ṣaṇmāsāṃś ca payasā bhojayej jāṅgalarasena vā, tatas trīn māsān ardhodakena
            payasā phalāmlena jāṅgalarasena vā, avaśiṣṭaṃ māsatrayam annaṃ laghu hitaṃ vā
            seveta, evaṃ saṃvatsareṇāgado bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.19"> bhavati cātra
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpane caiva virecane ca pāne tathā ''āhāravidhikriyāsu |
            <caesura/>
             sarvodaribhyaḥ kuśalaiḥ prayojyaṃ kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ jāṅgalajo raso vā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.14.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne udaracikitsitaṃ
            nāma caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||14 ||</l>
        </div>

        <div n="15" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.1"> athāto mūḍhagarbhacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.3"> nāto 'nyat kaṣṭatamamasti yathā
            mūḍhagarbhaśalyoddharaṇam; atra hi yoniyakṛtplīhāntravivaragarbhāśayānāṃ
            madhye karma kartavyaṃ sparśena,
            utkarṣaṇāpakarṣaṇasthānāpavartanotkartanabhedanacchedanapīḍanarjūkaraṇadāraṇāni
            caikahastena garbhaṃ garbhiṇīṃ cāhiṃsatā, tasmād adhipatimāpṛcchya paraṃ ca
            yatnamāsthāyopakrameta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.4"> tatra samāsenāṣṭavidhā mūḍhagarbhagatiruddiṣṭā;
            svabhāvagatā api trayaḥ saṅgā bhavanti śiraso vaiguṇyādaṃsayor jaghanasya vā
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.5"> jīvati tu garbhe sūtikāgarbhanirharaṇe prayateta |
            <caesura/>
             nirhartum aśakye cyāvanān mantrānupaśṛṇuyāt; tān vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.6"> ihāmṛtaṃ ca somaś ca citrabhānuś ca bhāmini |
            <caesura/>
             uccaiḥśravāś ca turago mandire nivasantu te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.7"> idamamṛtamapāṃ samuddhṛtaṃ vai tava laghu garbhamimaṃ
            pramuñcatu stri |
            <caesura/>
             tad analapavanārkavāsavās te saha lavaṇāmbudharair diśantu śāntim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.8"> muktāḥ paśorvipāśāś ca muktāḥ sūryeṇa raśmayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             muktaḥ sarvabhayād garbha ehyehi viramāvitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.9"> auṣadhāni ca vidadhyādyathoktāni | mṛte cottānāyā
            ābhugnasakthyā vastrādhārakonnamitakaṭhyā
            dhanvananagavṛttikāśālmalīmṛtsnaghṛtābhyāṃ mrakṣayitvā hastaṃ yonau praveśya
            garbham upaharet | tatra sakthibhyām āgatamanulomamevāñchet, ekasakthnā
            pratipannasyetarasakthi prasāryāpaharet, sphigdeśenāgatasya sphigdeśaṃ
            prapīḍyordhvam utkṣipya sakthinī prasāryāpaharet, tiryagāgatasya parighasyeva
            tiraścīnasya paś cād ardhamūrdhvamutkṣipya pūrvārdhamapatyapathaṃ
            pratyārjavamānīyāpaharet, pārśvāpavṛttaśirasamaṃsaṃ prapīḍyor dhvamutkṣipya
            śiro 'patyapatham ānīyāpaharet, bāhudvayapratipannasyor dhvamutpīḍyāṃsau śiro
            'nulomamānīyāpaharet, dvāvantyāvasādhyau mūḍhagarbhau, evamaśakye
            śastramavacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.10"> sacetanaṃ ca śastreṇa na kathañcana dārayet |
            <caesura/>
             dāryamāṇo hi jananīmātmānaṃ caiva ghātayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.11"> aviṣahye vikāre tu śreyo garbhasya pātanam |
            <caesura/>
             na garbhiṇyā viparyāsastasmāt prāptaṃ na hāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.12"> tataḥ striyamāśvāsya maṇḍalāgreṇāṅgulīśastreṇa vā śiro
            vidārya, śiraḥkapālānyāhṛtya, śaṅkunā gṛhītvorasi kakṣāyāṃ vā 'paharet;
            abhinnaśirasamakṣikūṭe gaṇḍe vā, aṃsasaṃsaktasyāṃsadeśe bāhū chittvā,
            dṛtimivātataṃ vātapūrṇodaraṃ vā vidārya nirasyāntrāṇi śithilībhūtamāharet,
            jaghanasaktasya vā jaghanakapālānīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.13"> kiṃbahunā yadyadaṅgaṃ hi garbhasya tasya sajjati
            tadbhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             samyagvinirharecchittvā rakṣennārīṃ ca yatnataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.14"> garbhasya gatayaś citrā jāyante 'nilakopataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tatrānalpamatirvaidyo varteta vidhipūrvakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.15"> nopekṣeta mṛtaṃ garbhaṃ muhūrtam api paṇḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sa hyāśu jananīṃ hanti nirucchvāsaṃ paśuṃ yathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.16"> maṇḍalāgreṇa kartavyaṃ chedyam antarvijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             vṛddhipatraṃ hi tīkṣṇāgraṃ nārīṃ hiṃsyāt kadācana || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.17"> athāpatantīm aparāṃ pātayet pūrvavad bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             hastenāpahared vā 'pi pārśvabhyāṃ paripīḍya vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.18"> dhunuyāc ca muhurnārīṃ pīḍayed vā 'ṃsapiṇḍikām |
            <caesura/>
             tailāktayonerevaṃ tāṃ pātayenmatimān bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.19"> evaṃ nirhṛtaśalyāṃ tu siñced uṣṇena vāriṇā |
            <caesura/>
             tato 'bhyaktaśarīrāyā yonau snehaṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.20"> evaṃ mṛdvī bhaved yonistacchūlaṃ copaśāmyati |
            <caesura/>
             kṛṣṇātanmūlaśuṇṭhyelāhiṅgubhārgīḥ sadīpyakāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.21"> vacāmativiṣāṃ rāsnāṃ cavyaṃ saṃcūrṇya pāyayet |
            <caesura/>
             snehena doṣasyandārthaṃ vedanopaśamāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.22"> kvāthaṃ caiṣāṃ tathā kalkaṃ cūrṇaṃ vā snehavarjitam |
            <caesura/>
             śākatvagghiṅgvativiṣāpāṭhākaṭukarohiṇīḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.23"> tathā tejovatīṃ cāpi pāyayet pūrvavadbhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             trirātraṃ pañcasaptāhaṃ tataḥ snehaṃ punaḥ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.24"> pāyayet āsavaṃ naktam ariṣṭaṃ vā susaṃskṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             śirīṣakakubhābhyāṃ ca toyam ācamane hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.25"> upadravāś ca ye 'nye syustān yathāsvamupācaret |
            <caesura/>
             sarvataḥ pariśuddhā ca snigdhapathyālpabhojanā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.26"> svedābhyaṅgaparā nityaṃ bhavet krodhavivarjitā |
            <caesura/>
             payo vātaharaiḥ siddhaṃ daśāhaṃ bhojane hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.27"> rasaṃ daśāhaṃ śeṣe tu yathāyogamupācaret |
            <caesura/>
             vyupadravāṃ viśuddhāṃ ca jñātvā ca varavarṇinīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.28"> ūrdhvaṃ caturbhyo māsebhyo visṛjet parihārataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yonisantarpaṇe 'bhyaṅge pāne bastiṣu bhojane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.29"> balātailamidaṃ cāsyai dadyādanilavāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             balāmūlakaṣāyasya daśamūlīśṛtasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.30"> yavakolakulatthānāṃ kvāthasya payasas tathā |
            <caesura/>
             aṣṭāvaṣṭau śubhā bhāgāstailādekastadekataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.31"> pacedāvāpya madhuraṃ gaṇaṃ saindhavasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             tathā 'guruṃ sarjarasaṃ saralaṃ devadāru ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.32"> mañjiṣṭhāṃ candanaṃ kuṣṭhamelāṃ kālānusārivām |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsīṃ śaileyakaṃ patraṃ tagaraṃ sārivāṃ vacām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.33"> śatāvarīmaśvagandhāṃ śatapuṣpāṃ punarnavām |
            <caesura/>
             tat sādhusiddhaṃ sauvarṇe rājate mṛnmaye 'pi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.34"> prakṣipya kalaśe samyak svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             balātailamidaṃ khyātaṃ sarvavātavikāranut || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.35"> yathābalamato mātrāṃ sūtikāyai pradāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             yā ca garbhārthinī nārī kṣīṇaśukraś ca yaḥ pumān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.36"> vātakṣīṇe marmahate mathite 'bhihate tathā |
            <caesura/>
             bhagne śramābhipanne ca sarvathaivopayujyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.37"> etad ākṣepakādīn vai vātavyādhīn apohati |
            <caesura/>
             hikkāṃ kāsamadhīmanthaṃ gulmaṃ śvāsaṃ ca dustaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.38"> ṣaṇmāsān upayujyaitad antravṛddhim apohati |
            <caesura/>
             pratyagradhātuḥ puruṣo bhavec ca sthirayauvanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.39"> rājñām etad dhi kartavyaṃ rājamātrāś ca ye narāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sukhinaḥ sukumārāś ca dhaninaś cāpi ye narāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.40"> balākaṣāyapītebhyas tilebhyo vā 'py anekaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tailam utpādya ||
            <caesura/>
             tat kvāthaśatapākaṃ kṛtaṃ śubham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.41"> nivāte nibhṛtāgāre prayuñjīta yathābalam | jīrṇe 'smin
            payasā snigdham aśnīyāt ṣaṣṭikaudanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.42"> anena vidhinā droṇam upayujyānnamīritam | bhuñjīta
            dviguṇaṃ kālaṃ balavarṇānvitas tataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.43"> sarvapāpair vinirmuktaḥ śatāyuḥ puruṣo bhavet | śataṃ
            śataṃ tathotkarṣo droṇe droṇe prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.44"> balākalpenātibalāguḍūcyādityaparṇiṣu | saireyake
            vīratarau śatāvaryāṃ trikaṇṭake || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.45"> tailāni madhuke kuryāt prasāriṇyāṃ ca buddhimān |
            nīlotpalaṃ varīmūlaṃ gavye kṣīre vipācayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.46"> śatapākaṃ tatas tena tilatailaṃ paced bhiṣak |
            balātailasya kalkāṃs tu supiṣṭāṃs tatra dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.47"> sarveṣām eva jānīyād upayogaṃ cikitsakaḥ | balātailavad
            eteṣāṃ guṇāṃś caiva viśeṣataḥ ||</l>

          <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne mūḍhagarbhacikitsitaṃ nāma
            pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||15 ||</trailer>
        </div>


        <div n="16" subtype="adhyāyaḥ" type="level2">
          <head>ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.1"> athāto vidradhītāṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.3"> ukta vidradhayaḥ ṣaḍye teṣv asādhyas tu sarvajaḥ |
            śeṣeṣvām eṣu kartavyā tvaritaṃ śophavat kriyā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.4"> vātaghnamūlakalkais tu ghṛtatailavasāyutaiḥ | sukhoṣṇo
            bahalo lepaḥ prayojyo vātavidradhau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.5"> sānūpaudakamāṃsas tu kākolyādiḥ satarpaṇaḥ |
            snehāmlasiddho lavaṇaḥ prayojyaś copanāhane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.6"> veśavāraiḥ sakṛśaraiḥ payobhiḥ pāyasais tathā | svedayet
            satataṃ cāpi nirharec cāpi śoṇitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.7"> sa ced evam upakrāntaḥ pākāyābhimukho yadi | taṃ
            pācayitvā śastreṇa bhindyād bhinnaṃ ca śodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.8"> pañcamūlakaṣāyeṇa prakṣālya lavaṇottaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tailair bhadrādimadhukasaṃyuktaiḥ pratipūrayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.9"> vair ecanikayuktena traivṛtena viśodhya ca |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthakparṇyādisiddhena traivṛtena ca ropayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.10"> paittikaṃ śarkarālājāmadhukaiḥ sārivāyutaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pradihyāt kṣīrapiṣṭair vā payasyośīracandanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.11"> pākyaiḥ śītakaṣāyair vā kṣīrair ikṣurasais tathā |
            <caesura/>
             jīvanīyaghṛtair vā 'pi secayec charkarāyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.12"> trivṛddharītakīnāṃ ca cūrṇaṃ lihyānmadhudravam |
            <caesura/>
             jalaukobhir hareccāsṛk pakvaṃ cāpaṭhya buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.13"> kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyeṇa prakṣālyaudakajena vā |
            <caesura/>
             tilaiḥ sayaṣṭīmadhukaiḥ sakṣaudraiḥ sarpiṣā yutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.14"> upadihya pratanunā vāsasā veṣṭayed vraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             prapauṇḍarīkamañjiṣṭhāmadhukośīrapadmakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.15"> saharidraiḥ kṛtaṃ sarpiḥ sakṣīraṃ vraṇaropaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīraśuklāpṛthakparṇīsamaṅgārodhracandanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.16"> nyagrodhādipravāleṣu teṣāṃ tvakṣvathavā kṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             naktamālasya patrāṇi taruṇāni phalāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.17"> sumanāyāś ca patrāṇi paṭolāriṣṭayos tathā |
            <caesura/>
             dve haridre madhūcchiṣṭaṃ madhukaṃ tiktarohiṇī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.18"> priyaṅguḥ kuśamūlaṃ ca niculasya tvageva ca |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhācandanośīramutpalaṃ sārive trivṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.19"> eteṣāṃ kārṣikair bhāgair ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭavraṇapraśamanaṃ nāḍīvraṇaviśodhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.20"> sadyaś chinnavraṇānāṃ ca karañjādyamidaṃ śubham |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭavraṇāś ca ye kecidye cotsṛṣṭakriyā vraṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.21"> nāḍyo gambhīrikā yāś ca sadyaś cchinnās tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             agnikṣārakṛtāś caiva ye vraṇā dāruṇā api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.22"> karañjādyena haviṣā praśāmyanti na saṃśayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             iṣṭakāsikatāloṣṭagośakṛttuṣapāṃśubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.23"> mūtrair uṣṇaiś ca satataṃ svedayec chlaṣmavidradhim |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyapānair vamanair ālepair upanāhanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.24"> hared doṣānabhīkṣṇaṃ cāpy alābvā 'sṛk tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             āragvadhakaṣāyeṇa pakvaṃ cāpāṭhya dhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.25"> haridrātrivṛtāśaktutilair madhusamāyutaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrayitvā vraṇaṃ samyagbadhnīyāt kīrtitaṃ yathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.26"> tataḥ kulatthikādantītrivṛcchyāmārkatilvakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kuryāt tailaṃ sagomūtraṃ hitaṃ tatra sasaindhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.27"> pittavidradhivat sarvāḥ kriyā niravaśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vidradhyoḥ kuśalaḥ kuryād raktāgantunimittayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.28"> varuṇādigaṇakvāthamapakve 'bhyantarotthite |
            <caesura/>
             ūṣakādipratīvāpaṃ pibet sukhakaraṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.29"> anayor vargayoḥ siddhaṃ sarpirvair ecanena ca |
            <caesura/>
             acirādvidradhiṃ hanti prātaḥ prātar niṣevitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.30"> ebhir eva gaṇaiś cāpi saṃsiddhaṃ snehasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             kāryamāsthāpanaṃ kṣipraṃ tathaivāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.31"> pānālepanabhojyeṣu madhuśigrudrumo 'pi vā |
            <caesura/>
             dattāvāpo yathādoṣamapakvaṃ hanti vidradhim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.32"> toyadhānyāmlamūtrais tu peyo vā 'pi surādibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathādoṣagaṇakvāthaiḥ pibed vā 'pi śilājatu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.33"> pradhānaṃ guggulaṃ cāpi śuṇṭhīṃ ca suradāru ca |
            <caesura/>
             snehopanāhau kuryāc ca sadā cāpy anulomanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.34"> yathoddiṣṭāṃ sirāṃ vidhyet kaphaje vidradhau bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             raktapittānilottheṣu kecidbāhau vadanti tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.35"> pakvaṃ vā bahirunnaddhaṃ bhittvā vraṇavadācaret |
            <caesura/>
             sruteṣūrdhvamadho vā 'pi mair eyāmlasurāsavaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.36"> peyo varuṇakādis tu madhuśigrudrumo 'pi vā |
            <caesura/>
             śigrumūlajale siddhaṃ sasiddhārthakam odanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.37"> yavakolakulatthānāṃ yūṣair bhuñjīta mānavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prātaḥ prātaś ca seveta mātrayā tailvakaṃ ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.38"> trivṛtādigaṇakvāthasiddhaṃ vā 'pyupaśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             nopagacched yathāpākaṃ prayateta tathā bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.39"> paryāgate vidradhau tu siddhirnaikāntikī smṛtā |
            <caesura/>
             pratyākhyāya tu kurvīta majjajāte tu vidradhau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.40"> snehasvedopapannānāṃ kuryād raktāvasecana |
            <caesura/>
             vidradhyuktāṃ kriyāṃ kuryāt pakve vā 'sthi tu bhedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.41"> niḥśalyamatha vijñāya kartavyaṃ vraṇaśodhanam |
            <caesura/>
             dhāvettiktakaṣāyeṇa tiktaṃ sarpis tathā hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.42"> yadi majjaparisrāvo na nivarteta dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kuryāt saṃśodhanīyāni kaṣāyādīni buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.16.43"> priyaṅgudhātakīrodhrakaṭphalaṃ tinisaindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             etais tailaṃ vipaktavyaṃ vidradhivraṇaropaṇam ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne vidradhicikitsitaṃ nāma
            ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||16 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="17" type="adhyāya">
          <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.1"> athāto visarpanāḍīstanarogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.3"> sādhyā visarpāstraya ādito ye na sannipātakṣatajau hi
            sādhyau |
            <caesura/>
             sādhyeṣu tatpathyagaṇair vidadhyād ghṛtāni sekāṃś ca tathopadehān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.4"> mustāśatāhvāsuradārukuṣṭhavārāhikustumburukṛṣṇagandhāḥ |
            vātātmako coṣṇagaṇāḥ prayojyāḥ sekeṣu lepeṣu tathā sadantīn
            surāṣṭrajāsaindhavasaṃprayuktān | prakṣālane cāpi
            karañjanimbajātyakṣapīlusvarasāḥ prayojyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.5"> yat pañcamūlaṃ khalu kaṇṭakākhyamalpaṃ mahac cāpy atha
            vallijaṃ ca| taccopayojyaṃ bhiṣajā pardehe seke ghṛte cāpi tathaiva taile|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.6"> kaseruśṛṅgāṭakapadmagundrāḥ saśaivalāḥ sotpalakardamāśca|
            vastrāntarāḥ pittakṛte visarpe lepā vidheyāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītāḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.7"> hrīveralāmajjakacandanāni srotojamuktāmaṇigairikāśca|
            kṣīreṇa piṣṭāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītā lepāḥ prayojyāstanavaḥ sukhāya|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.8"> prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ payasyā mañjiṣṭhikā
            padmakacandane ca| sugandhikā ceti sukhāya lepaḥ paitte visarpe bhiṣajā
            prayojyaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.9"> nyagrodhavargaiḥ pariṣecanaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ ca kuryāt
            svarasena tasya| śītaiḥ payo bhiś ca madhūdakaiśca saśarkarairikṣurasaiś ca
            sekān|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.10"> ghṛtasya gaurīmadhukāravindarodhrāmburājādanagairikeṣu|
            tatharṣabhe padmakasārivāsu kākolimedākumudotpaleṣu|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.11"> sacandanāyāṃ madhuśarkarāyāṃ
            drākṣāsthirāpṛśniśatāhvayāsu| kalkīkṛtāsūdakamatra dattvā nyagrodhavargasya
            tathā sthirādeḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.12"> gaṇasya bilvādikapañcamūlyāścaturguṇaṃ kṣīramathāpi
            tadvat| prasthaṃ vipakvaṃ pariṣecanena paittīrnihanyāt tu visarpanāḍīḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.13"> visphoṭaduṣṭavraṇaśīrṣarogān pākaṃ tathā++āsyasya
            nihanti pānāt| grahārdite śoṣiṇi cāpi bāle ghṛtaṃ hi gauryādikametadiṣṭam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.14"> ajā+aśvagandhā saralā sakālā saikaiṣikā cāpy
            athavā+ajaśṛṅgī| gomūtrapiṣṭo vihitaḥ pradeho hanyādvisarpaṃ kaphajaṃ sa
            śīghram|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.15"> kālānusāryāgurucocaguñjārāsnāvacāśītaśivedraparṇyaḥ|
            pālindimuñjātamahīkadambā hitā visarpeṣu kaphātmakeṣu|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.16"> gaṇas tu yojyo varuṇapravṛttaḥ kriyāsu sarvāsu
            vicakṣaṇena| saṃśodhanaṃ śoṇitamokṣaṇaṃ ca śreṣṭhaṃ visarpeṣu cikitsitaṃ hi|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.17"> sarvāṃś ca pakvān pariśodhya dhīmān vraṇakrameṇopacared
            yathoktam| nāḍī tridoṣaprabhavā na sidhyeccheṣāścatasraḥ khalu yatnasādhyāḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.18"> tatrānilotthām upanāhya pūrvamaśeṣataḥ pūyagatiṃ
            vidārya| tilairapāmārgaphalaiś ca piṣṭvā sasaindhavairbandhanamatra kuryāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.19"> prakṣālane cāpi sadā varaṇasya yojyaṃ mahadyat khalu
            pañcamūlam| hiṃsrāṃ haridrāṃ kaṭukāṃ balāṃ ca gojihvikāṃ cāpi sabilvamūlām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.20"> saṃhṛtya tailaṃ vipaced vraṇasya saṃśodhanaṃ
            pūraṇaropaṇaṃ ca| pittātmikāṃ prāgupanāhya dhīmānutkārikābhiḥ
            sapayoghṛtābhiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.21"> nipātya śastraṃ tilanāgadantīyaṣṭyāhvakalkaiḥ
            paripūrayettām| prakṣālane cāpi sasomanimbā niśā prayojyā kuśalena nityam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.22"> śyāmātribhaṇḍītriphalāsu siddhaṃ haridrayo
            rodhrakavṛkṣayośca| ghṛtaṃ sadugdhaṃ vraṇatarpaṇena hanyād gatiṃ
            koṣṭhagatā+api yā syāt|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.23"> nāḍīṃ kaphotthām upanāhya samyak
            kulatthasiddhārthakaśaktukiṇvaiḥ| mṛdūkṛtāmeṣya gatiṃ viditvā nipātayec
            chastramaśeṣakārī|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.24"> dadyādvraṇe nimbatilān sadantīn
            surāṣṭrajāsaindhavasaṃprayuktān| prakṣālane cāpi
            karañjanimbajātyakṣapīlusvarasāḥ prayojyāḥ|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.25"> suvarcikāsaindhavacitrakeṣu nikumbhatālītalarūpikāsu |
            <caesura/>
             phaleṣv apāmārgabhaveṣu caiva kuryāt samūtreṣu hitāya tailam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.26"> nāḍīṃ tu śalyaprabhavāṃ vidārya nirhṛtya śalyaṃ
            praviśodhya mārgam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃśodhayet kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhais tilais tato ropaṇamāśu kuryāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.27"> kumbhīkakharjūrakapitthabilvavanaspatīnāṃ ca
            śalāṭuvargaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ vipacet tu tailamāvāpya mustāsaralāpriyaṅgūḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.28"> sugandhikāmocarasāhipuṣoaṃ rodhraṃ vidadhyādapi dhātakīṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             etena śalyaprabhavā tu nāḍī rohed vraṇo vā sukhabhāśu caiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.29"> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ nāḍī marmāśritā ca yā |
            <caesura/>
             kṣārasūtreṇa tāṃ cchindyān na tu śastreṇa buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.30"> eṣaṇyā gatimanviṣya ārasūtrānusāriṇīm |
            <caesura/>
             sūcīṃ nidadhyād gatyante tahonnamyāśu nirharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.31"> sūtrasyāntaṃ samānīya gāḍhaṃ bandhaṃ samācaret |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ kṣārabalaṃ vīkṣya sūtramanyat praveśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.32"> kṣārāktaṃ matimān vaidyo yāvanna chidyate gatiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhagandare 'pyeṣa vidhiḥ kāryo vaidyena jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.33"> sūcībhir yavavaktrābhir ācitān vā samantataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūle sūtreṇa badhnīyācchinne copavared vraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.34"> yā dvivraṇīye 'bhihitās tu vartyastāḥ sarvanāḍīṣu
            bhiṣagvidadhyāt |
            <caesura/>
             ghoṇṭāphalatvaglavaṇāni lākṣāpūgīphalaṃ cālavaṇaṃ ca patram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.35"> sruhyarkadugdhena tu kalka eṣa vartīkṛto hantyacireṇa
            nāḍīḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bibhītakāmrāsthivaṭapravālā hareṇukāśaṅkhinibījamasyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.36"> vārāhikandaś ca tathā pradeyo nāḍīṣu tailena ca
            miśrayitvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.37"> dhattūrajaṃ madanakodravajaṃ ca bījaṃ kośātakī śukanasā
            mṛgabhojinī ca |
            <caesura/>
             aṅkoṭabījakusumaṃ gatiṣu prayojyaṃ lākṣodakāhṛtamalāsu vikṛtya cūrṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.38"> tathā ca gomāṃsamasīṃ hitāya koṣṭhāśritasyādarato
            diśanti |
            <caesura/>
             varīkṛtaṃ mākṣikasaṃprayuktaṃ nāḍīghnamuktaṃ lavaṇottamaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.39"> duṣṭavraṇe yadvihitaṃ ca tailaṃ tat sarvanāḍīṣu
            bhiṣagvidadhyāt |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇīkṛtair atha vimiśritamebhir eva tailaṃ prayuktamacireṇa gatiṃ nihanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.40"> eṣv eva mūtrasahiteṣu vidhāya tailaṃ tat sādhitaṃ gatim
            apohati saptarātrāt |
            <caesura/>
             piṇḍītakasya tu varāhavibhāvitasya mūleṣu kandaśakaleṣu ca sauvaheṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.41"> tailaṃ kṛtaṃ gatim apohati śīghrametat kandeṣu
            cāmaravarāyudhasāhvayeṣu |
            <caesura/>
             bhallātakārkamaricair lavaṇottamena siddhaṃ viḍaṅgarajanīdvayacitrakaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.42"> syan mārkavasya ca rasena nihanti tailaṃ nāḍīṃ
            kaphānilakṛtām apacīṃ vraṇāṃś ca |
            <caesura/>
             stanye gate vikṛtimāśu bhiṣak tu dhātrīṃ pītāṃ ghṛtaṃ pariṇate 'hani vāmayet
            tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.43"> nimbodakena madhumāgadhikāyutena vāntāgate 'hani ca
            mudgarasāśanā syāt |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃ tryahaṃ caturahaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ vamed vā sarpiḥ pibet triphalayā saha saṃyutaṃ
            vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.44"> bhārgīṃ pibet tu payasaḥ pariśodhanārtham āragvadhādiṣu
            varaṃ madhunā kaṣāyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.45"> sāmānyam etad upadiṣṭam ato viśeṣād doṣān payonipatitān
            śamayed yathāsvam |
            <caesura/>
             rogaṃ stanotthitam avekṣya bhiṣag vidadhyād yad vidradhāvabhihitaṃ bahuśo
            vidhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.46"> saṃpacyamānam api taṃ tu vinopanāhaiḥ saṃbhojanena khalu
            pācayituṃ yateta |
            <caesura/>
             śīghraṃ stano hi mṛdumāṃsatayopanaddhaḥ sarvaṃ prakotham upayāty avadīryate
            ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.47"> pakve tu dugdhahariṇīḥ parihṛtya nāḍīḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ca
            cūcukayugaṃ vidadhīta śastram |
            <caesura/>
             āme vidāhini tathaiva gate ca pākaṃ dhātryāḥ stanau satatam eva ca nirduhīta
            ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            visarpanāḍīstanarogacikitsitaṃ nāma saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||17 || </p>
        </div>


        <div n="18" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.1"> athāto granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3"> granthiṣvathāmeṣu bhiṣag vidadhyāc chophakriyāṃ
            vistaraśokāryāḥ pittārbude kāyavirecanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             vighṛṣya codumbaraśākagojīpatrair bhṛśaṃ kṣaudrayutaiḥ pralimpet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.4"> tailaṃ pibet sarpiratho dvayaṃ vā dattvā vasāṃ vā
            trivṛtaṃ vidadhyāt| apehivātādaśamūlasiddhaṃ vaidyaścatuḥsnehamatho dvayaṃ
            vā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.5"> hiṃsrā+atha rohiṇyamṛtā+atha bhargī
            śyonākabilvāgurukṛṣṇagandhāḥ| gojī ca piṣṭā saha tālapatryā granthau vidheyo
            'nilaje pralepaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.6"> svedopanāhān vividhāṃśca kuryāt tathā prasiddhānaparāṃś
            ca lepān| vidārya vā pakvamapohya pūyaṃ prakṣālya bilvārkanarendratoyaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.7"> tilaiḥ sapañcāṅgulapatramiśraiḥ saṃśodhayet
            saindhavasaṃprayuktaiḥ| śuddhaṃ vraṇaṃ vā+apyuparopayettu tailena
            rāsnāsaralānvitena|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.8"> viḍaṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāmṛtābhiḥ siddhena vā kṣīrasamanvitena|
            jalaukasaḥ pittakṛte hitās tu kṣīrodakābhyāṃ paribecanaṃ ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.9"> kākolivargasya ca śītalāni pibet kaṣāyāṇi saśarkarāṇi|
            drākṣārasenekṣurasena vā+api cūrṇaṃ pibeccāpi harītakīnām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.10"> madhūkajambvarjunavetasānāṃ tvagbhiḥ
            pradehānavacārayeta| saśarkarair vā tṛṇaśūnyakandairdihyādabhīkṣṇaṃ
            muculundajair vā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.11"> vidārya vā pakvamapohya pūyaṃ dhāvet kaṣāyeṇa
            vanaspatīnām| tilaiḥ sayaṣṭīmadhukair viśodhya sarpiḥ prayojyaṃ madhurair
            vipakvam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.12"> hṛteṣu doṣeṣu yathānupūrvyā granthau bhiṣak
            śleṣmasamutthite tu| svinnasya vimlāpanameva kuryād
            aṅguṣṭhalohopalaveṇudaṇḍaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.13"> vikaṅkatāragvadhakākaṇantīkākādanītāpasavṛkṣamūlaiḥ|
            ālepayet piṇḍaphalārkabhārgīkarañjakālāmadanaiś ca vidvān|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.14"> amarmajātaṃ śamamaprayāntamapakvamevāpaharedvidārya|
            dahet sthite cāsṛji siddhakarmā sadyaḥkṣatoktaṃ ca vidhiṃ vidadhyāt|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.15"> yā māṃsakandyaḥ kaṭhinā bṛhatyastāsveṣa yojyaś ca
            vidhirvidhijñaiḥ| śastreṇa vā++āpāṭhya supakvamāśu prakṣālayet pathyatamaiḥ
            kaṣāyaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.16"> saṃśodhanais taṃ ca viśodhayet tu kṣārottaraiḥ
            kṣaudraguḍapragāḍhaiḥ| śuddhe ca tailaṃ tvavacāraṇīyaṃ
            viḍaṅgapāṭhārajanīvipakvam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.17"> medaḥsamutthe tilakalkadigdhaṃ dattvopariṣṭādviguṇaṃ
            paṭāntam| hutāśataptena muhuḥ pramṛjyāllohena dhīmānadahan hitāya|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.18"> pralipya dārvīmatha lākṣayā vā prataptayā svedanamasya
            kāryam| nipātya vā śastramapohya medo dahet supakvaṃ tvathavā vidārya|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.19"> prakṣālya mūtreṇa tilaiḥ supiṣṭaiḥ
            suvarcikādyairharitālamiśraiḥ| sasaindhavaiḥ kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaiḥ
            kṣārottarairenamabhipraśodhya|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.20"> tailaṃ
            vidadyāddvikarañjaguñjāvaṃśāvalekheṅgudamūtrasiddham| jīmūtakaiḥ
            kośavatīphalaiś ca dantīdravantītrivṛtāsu caiva|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.21"> sarpiḥ kṛtaṃ hantyapacīṃ pravṛddhāṃ dvidhā pravṛttaṃ
            tadudāravīryam| nirguṇḍijātībarihiṣṭhayuktaṃ jīmūtakaṃ mākṣikasaindhavāḍhyam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.22"> abhiprataptaṃ vamanaṃ pragāḍhaṃ
            duṣṭāpacīṣūttamamādiśanti| kaiḍaryabimbīkaravīrasiddhaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ
            mūrdhavirecanaṃ ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.23"> śāsvoṭakasya svarasena siddhaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ
            nasyavirecaneṣu| madhūkasāraś ca hito 'vapīḍe phalāni śigroḥ kharamañjarervā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.24"> granthīnamarmaprabhavānapakvānuddhṛtya cāgniṃ vidadhīta
            paścāt| kṣāreṇa vā+api pratisārayet tu saṃlikhya śastreṇa yathopadeśam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.25"> pārṣṇi prati dve daśa cāṅgulāni mitvendrabastiṃ
            parivarjya dhīmān| vidārya matsyāṇḍanibhāni vaidyo niṣkṛṣya jālānyanalaṃ
            vidadhyāt|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.26"> ā gulphakarṇāt sumitasya jantostasyāṣṭabhāgaṃ
            khuḍakādvibhajya| ghoṇarjuvedhaḥ surarājabasterhitvā+akṣimātraṃ tvapare
            vadanti|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.27"> maṇibandhopariṣṭādvā kuryād rekhātrayaṃ bhiṣak|
            aṅgulyantaritaṃ samyagapacīnāṃ nivṛttaye|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.28"> cūrṇasya kāle parcalākakākagodhāhikūrmaprabhavāṃ masīṃ
            tu| dadyāc ca tailena saheṅgudīnāṃ yadvakṣyate ślīpadināṃ ca tailam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.29"> virecanaṃ dhūmamupādadīta bhavec ca nityaṃ
            yavamudgabhojī| karkārukair vārukanāsirkelapriyālapañcāṅgulabījacūrṇaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.30"> vātārbudaṃ kṣīraghṛtāmbusiddhair uṣṇaiḥ satailair
            upanāhayettu| kuryāc ca mukhyānyupanāhanāni siddhaiś ca māṃsairatha
            vesavāraiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.31"> svedaṃ vidadhyāt kuśalastu nāḍyā śṛṅgeṇa raktaṃ bahuśo
            harec ca| vātaghnaniryūhapayomlabhāgaiḥ siddhaṃ śatākhyaṃ trivṛtaṃ pibed vā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.32"> svedopanāhā mṛdavas tu kāryāḥ pittārbude kāyavirecanaṃ
            ca| vighṛṣya codumbaraśākagojīpatrairbhṛśaṃ kṣaudrayutaiḥ pralimpet|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.33"> ślakṣṇīkṛtaiḥ
            sarjarasapriyaṅgupattaṅgarodhrāñjanayaṣṭikāhvaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             visrāvya cāragvadhāgojisomāḥ śyāmā ca yojyā kuśalena lepe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.34"> śyāmāgirihvāñjanakīraseṣu drākṣārase saptalikārase ca |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaṃ pibet klītakasaṃprasiddhaṃ pittārbudī tajjaṭharī ca jantuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.35"> śuddhasya jantoḥ kaphaje 'rbude tu rakte 'vasikte tu
            tato 'rbudaṃ tat |
            <caesura/>
             dravyāṇi yānyūrdhvamadhaś ca doṣān haranti taiḥ kalkakṛtaiḥ pradihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.36"> kapotapārāvataviṅvimiśraiḥ sakāṃsyanīlaiḥ
            śukalāṅgalākhyaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrais tu kākādanimūlamiśraiḥ kṣārapradigdhair athavā pradihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.37"> niṣpāvapiṇyākakulatthakalkair māṃsapragāḍhair
            dadhimastuyuktaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lepaṃ vidadhyāt kṛmayo yathā 'tra mūrcchanti muñcantyatha makṣikāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.38"> alpāvaśiṣṭe kṛmibhakṣite ca likhettato 'gniṃ vidadhīta
            paś cāt |
            <caesura/>
             yadalpamūlaṃ traputāmrasīsapaṭṭaiḥ samāveṣṭya tadāyasair vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.39"> kṣārāgniśastrāṇyasakṛdvidadhyāt prāṇānahiṃsan
            bhiṣagpramattaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āsphotajātīkaravīrapatraiḥ kaṣāyamiṣṭaṃ vraṇaśodhanārtham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.40"> śuddhe ca tailaṃ vidadhīta
            bhārgīviḍaṅgapāṭhātriphalāvipakvam |
            <caesura/>
             yadṛcchayā copagatāni pākaṃ pākakrameṇopacared vidhijñaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.41"> medorbudaṃ svinnamatho vidārya viśodhya sīvyed
            gataraktam āśu |
            <caesura/>
             tato haridrāgṛhadhūmarodhrapataṅgacūrṇaiḥ samanaḥ śilālaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.42"> vraṇaṃ pratigrāhya madhupragāḍhaiḥ karañjatailaṃ
            vidadhīta śuddhe |
            <caesura/>
             saśeṣadoṣāṇi hi yo 'rbudāni karoti tasyāśu punarbhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.43"> tasmād aśeṣāṇi samuddharet tu hanyuḥ saśeṣāṇi yathā hi
            vahniḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃsvedya gaṇḍaṃ pavanotthamādau nāḍyā 'nilaghnauṣadhapatrabhaṅgaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.44"> amlaiḥ samūtrair vividhaiḥ payobhir uṣṇaiḥ satailaiḥ
            piśitaiś ca vidvān |
            <caesura/>
             visrāvayet svinnamatandriyaś ca śuddhaṃ vraṇaṃ cāpy upanāhayet tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.45"> śaṇātasīmūlakaśigrukiṇvapriyālamajjānuyutais tilais tu |
            <caesura/>
             kālāmṛtāśigrupunarnavārkagajādināmākarahāṭakuṣṭhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.46"> ekaiṣikāvṛkṣakatilvakaiś ca surāmlapiṣṭair asakṛt
            pradihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.47"> tailaṃ pibeccāmṛtavallinimbahaṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.48"> svedopanāhaiḥ kaphasaṃbhavaṃ tu saṃsvedaya visrāvaṇam
            eva kuryāt |
            <caesura/>
             tato 'jagandhātiviṣāviśalyāviṣāṇikākuṣṭhaśukāhvayābhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.49"> palāśabhasmodakapeṣitābhir dihyāt suguñjābhir
            aśītalābhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             daśārdhasaṅkhyair lavaṇaiś ca yuktaṃ tailaṃ pibenmāgadhikādisiddham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.50"> pracchardanaṃ mūrdhavirecanaṃ ca dhūmaś ca vair ecaniko
            hitas tu |
            <caesura/>
             pākakramo vā 'pi sadā vidheyo vaidyena pākaṅgatayoḥ kathañcit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.51"> kaṭutrikakṣaudrayutāḥ samūtrā bhakṣyā yavānnāni rasāś ca
            maudgāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśṛṅgaverāḥ sapaṭolanimbā hitāya deyā galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.52"> medaḥsamutthe tu yathopadiṣṭāṃ vidhyet sirāṃ
            snigdhatanornarasya |
            <caesura/>
             śyāmāsudhālohapurīṣadantīrasāñjanaiś cāpi hitaḥ pradehaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.53"> mūtreṇa vā+āloḍya hitāya sāraṃ prātaḥ pibet
            sālamahīruhāṇām |
            <caesura/>
             śastreṇa vā ''āpāṭya vidārya cainaṃ medaḥ samuddhṛtya hitāya sīvyet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.54"> majjājyamedomadhubhir dahed vā dagdhe ca sarpirmadhu
            cāvacāryam |
            <caesura/>
             kāsīsatutthe ca tato 'tra deye cūrṇīkṛte rocanayā samete || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.55"> tailena cābhyajya hitāya dadyāt sārodbhavaṃ gomayajaṃ ca
            bhasma |
            <caesura/>
             hitaś ca nityaṃ triphalākaṣāyo gāḍhaś ca bandho yavabhojanaṃ ca ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍacikitsitaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||18 ||</p>
        </div>



        <div n="19" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.1"> athāto vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpadacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.3"> antravṛddhyā vinā ṣaḍyā vṛddhayas tāsu varjayet |
            <caesura/>
             aśvādiyānaṃ vyāyāmaṃ maithunaṃ veganigraham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.4"> atyāsanaṃ caṅkramaṇam upavāsaṃ gurūṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             tatrādito vātavṛddhau traivṛtasnigdhamāturam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.5"> svinnaṃ cainaṃ yathānyāyaṃ pāyayeta virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"> sakṣīraṃ vā pibenmāsaṃ tailameraṇḍasaṃbhavam |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.7"> nirūhayen nirūḍhaṃ ca bhuktavantaṃ rasaudanam |
            <caesura/>
             yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tatas tailena yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.8"> snehopanāhau kuryāc ca pradehāṃś cānilāpahān |
            <caesura/>
             vidagdhāṃ pācayitvā vā sevanīṃ parivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.9"> bhindyāttataḥ prabhinnāyāṃ yathoktaṃ kramam ācaret |
            <caesura/>
             pittajāyāmapakvāyāṃ pittagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.10"> pakvāṃ vā bhedayed bhinnāṃ śodhayet kṣaudrasarpiṣā |
            <caesura/>
             śuddhāyāṃ ca bhiṣagdadyāttailaṃ kalkaṃ ca ropaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.11"> raktajāyāṃ jalaukobhiḥ śoṇitaṃ nirhared bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             pibed virecanaṃ vā 'pi śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.12"> pittagranthikramaṃ kuryād āme pakve ca sarvadā |
            <caesura/>
             vṛddhiṃ kaphātmikāmuṣṇair mūtrapiṣṭaiḥ pralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.13"> pītadārukaṣāyaṃ ca piben mūtreṇa saṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             vimlāpanād ṛte vā 'pi śleṣmagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.14"> pakvāyāṃ ca vibhinnāyāṃ tailaṃ śodhanamiṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             sumanāruṣkarāṅkoṭhasaptaparṇeṣu sādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.15"> medaḥsamutthāṃ saṃsvedya lepayet surasādinā |
            <caesura/>
             śirovirekadravyair vā sukhoṣṇair mūtrasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.16"> svinnāṃ cāveṣṭya paṭṭena samāśvāsya tu mānavam |
            <caesura/>
             rakṣan phale sevanīṃ ca vṛddhipatreṇa dārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.17"> medas tataḥ samuddhṛtya dadyāt kāsīsasaindhave |
            <caesura/>
             badhnīyāc ca yathoddiṣṭaṃ śuddhe tailaṃ ca dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.18"> manaḥśilālalavaṇaiḥ siddhamāruṣkareṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrajāṃ svedayitvā tu vastrapaṭṭena veṣṭayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.19"> sevanyāḥ pārśvato 'dhastād vidhyed vrīhimukhena tu |
            <caesura/>
             athātra dvimukhāṃ nāḍīṃ dattvā visrāvayed bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.20"> mūtraṃ nāḍīm athoddhṛtya sthagikābandham ācaret |
            <caesura/>
             śuddhāyāṃ ropaṇaṃ dadyād varjayed antrahaitukīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.21"> aprāptaphalakoṣāyāṃ vātavṛddhikramo hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tatra yā vaṅkhaṇasthā tāṃ dahed ardhenduvattrayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.22"> samyaṅmārgāvarodhārthaṃ kośaprāptāṃ tu varjayet |
            <caesura/>
             tvacaṃ bhittvā 'ṅguṣṭhamadhye dahec cāṅgaviparyayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.23"> anenaiva vidhānena vṛddhī vātakaphātmike |
            <caesura/>
             pradahet prayataḥ kiṃ tu snāyucchedo 'dhikas tayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.24"> śaṅkhopari ca karṇānte tyaktvā yatnena sevanīm |
            <caesura/>
             vyatyāsādvā sirāṃ vidhyed antravṛddhinivṛttaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.25"> upadaṃśeṣu sādhyeṣu snigdhasvinnasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sirāṃ vidhyenmeḍhramadhye pātayed vā jalaukasaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.26"> hared ubhayataś cāpi doṣān atyartham ucchritān |
            <caesura/>
             sadyo 'pahṛtadoṣasya rukśophāv upaśāmyataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.27"> yadi vā durbalo jantur na vā prāptaṃ virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             nirūheṇa haret tasya doṣān atyartham ucchritān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.28"> prapauṇḍarīkayaṣṭyāhvavarṣābhūkuṣṭhadārubhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saralāgururāsnābhir vātajaṃ saṃpralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.29"> niculair aṇḍabījāni yavagodhūmasaktavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             etaiś ca vātajaṃ snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ saṃpralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.30"> prapauṇḍarīkapūrvaiś ca dravyaiḥ sekaḥ praśasyate |
            <caesura/>
             gaurikāñjanayaṣṭyāhvārivośīrapadmakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.31"> sacandanotpalaiḥ snigdhaiḥ paittikaṃ saṃpralepayet |
            <caesura/>
             padmotpalamṛṇālaiś ca sasarjārjunavetasaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.32"> sarpiḥsnigdhaiḥ samadhukaiḥ paittikaṃ saṃpralepayet |
            <caesura/>
             secayec ca ghṛtakṣīraśarkarekṣumadhūdakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.33"> athavā 'pi suśītena kaṣāyeṇa vaṭādinā |
            <caesura/>
             sālāśvakarṇājakarṇadhavatvagbhiḥ kaphotthitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.34"> surāpiṣṭābhir uṣṇābhiḥ satailābhiḥ pralepayet |
            <caesura/>
             rajanyativiṣāmustāsurāsuradārubhiḥ || </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.35"> saptrapāṭhāpattūrairathavā saṃpralepayet|
            surasāragvadhādyoś ca kvāthābhyāṃ paribecayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.36"> evaṃ saṃśodhanālepasekaśoṇitamokṣaṇaiḥ| pratikuryāt
            kriyāyogaiḥ prāksthānoktairhitairapi|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.37"> na yāti ca yathā pākaṃ prayateta tathā bhiṣak|
            vidagdhais tu sirāsnāyutvaṅmāṃsaiḥ kṣīyate dhvajaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.38"> śastreṇopacareccāpi pākamāgatamāśu vai| tadā+apohya
            tilaiḥ sarpiḥkṣaudrayuktaiḥ pralepayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.39"> karavīrasya patrāṇi jātyāragvadhayostathā| prakṣālane
            prayojyāni vaijayantyarkayor api|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.40"> saurāṣṭrīṃ gairikaṃ tutthaṃ puṣpakāsīsasaindhavam|
            rodhraṃ rasāñjanaṃ dārvīṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.41"> hareṇukaile ca tathā sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet| taccūrṇaṃ
            kṣaudrasaṃyuktam upadaṃśeṣu pūjitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.42"> jambvāmrasumanānimbaśvetakāmbojipallavāḥ|
            śallakībadarībilvapalāśatiniśatvacaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.43"> kṣīriṇāṃ ca tvaco yojyāḥ kvāthe triphalayā saha| tena
            kvāthena niyataṃ vraṇaṃ prākṣālayed bhiṣak|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.44"> asminn eva kaṣāye tu tailaṃ dhīro vipācayet |
            gojīviḍaṅgayaṣṭībhiḥ sarvagandhaiś ca saṃyutam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.45"> etat sarvopadaṃśeṣu śreṣṭhaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate|
            svarjikātutthakāsīsaṃ śaileyaṃ ca rasāñjanam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.46"> manaḥśilāsamaiś cūrṇaṃ vraṇavīsśarpanāśanam| gundrāṃ
            dagdhvā kṛtaṃ bhasma haritālaṃ manaḥśilā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.47"> upadaṃśabisarpāṇāmetacchantikaraṃ param|
            mārkavastriphalā dantī tāmracūrṇamayor ajaḥ|| a</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.48"> upadaṃśaṃ nihanty eṣa vṛkṣam indrāśanir yathā| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.48b"> upadaṃśadvaye+apyetāṃ pratyākhyāyācaret kriyām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.49"> tayor eva ca yā yogyā vīkṣya doṣabalābalam| upadaṃśe
            viśeṣeṇa śṛṇu bhūyastridoṣaje|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.50"> duṣṭavraṇavidhiṃ kuryāt kuthitaṃ mehanaṃ tyajet|
            jambvoṣṭhenāgnivarṇena paś cāccheṣaṃ dahed bhiṣak|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.51"> samyagdagdhaṃ ca vijñāya madhusarpiḥ prayojayet| śuddhe
            ca ropaṇaṃ dadyāt kalkaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ ca yat|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.52"> snehasvedopapanne tu ślīpade+anilane bhiṣak| kṛtvā
            gulphopari sirāṃ vidhyet tu caturaṅgule|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.53"> samāpyāyitadehaṃ ca bastibhiḥ samupācaret|
            māsameraṇḍajaṃ tailaṃ pibenmūtreṇa saṃyutam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.54"> payasaudanamaśnīyānnāgarakvathitena ca| taivṛtaṃ
            copayuñjīta śasto dāhastathā+agninā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.55"> gulphasyādhaḥ sirāṃ vidhyecchlīpade pittasaṃbhave|
            pītaghnīṃ ca kriyāṃ kuryāt pittārbudavisarpavat|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.56"> sirāṃ suviditāṃ vidhyed aṅguṣṭhe ślaiṣmike bhiṣak|
            madhuyuktāni cābhīkṣṇaṃ kaṣāyāṇi piben naraḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.57"> pibed vā+apyabhayākalkaṃ mūtreṇānyatamena ca|
            kaṭukāmamṛtāṃ śuṇṭhīṃ viḍaṅgaṃ dāru citrakam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.58"> hitaṃ vā lepane nityaṃ bhadradāru sacitrakam|
            viḍaṅgamaricārkeṣu nāgare citrake+athavā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.59"> bhadradārvelukākhye ca sarveṣu lavaṇeṣu ca| tailaṃ
            pakvaṃ pibed vā+api yavānnaṃ ca hitaṃ sadā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.60"> pibet sarṣapatailaṃ vā ślīpadānāṃ nivṛttaye|
            pūtīkarañjapatrāṇāṃ rasaṃ vā+api yathābalam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.61"> anenaiva vidhānena putrañjīvakajaṃ rasam| prayuñjīta
            bhiṣak prājñaḥ kālasātmyavibhāgavit|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.62"> kevukākandaniryāsaṃ lavaṇaṃ tvatha pākimam| rasaṃ
            dattvā+atha pūrvoktaṃ peyametadbhiṣagjitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.63"> kākādanīṃ kākajaṅghāṃ bṛhatīṃ kaṇṭakārikām|
            kadambapuṣpīṃ mandārīṃ lambāṃ śukanasāṃ tathā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.64"> dagdhvā mūtreṇa tadbhasma srāvayet kṣārakalpavat| tatra
            dadyāt pratīvāpaṃ kākodumbarikārasam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.65"> madanāc ca phalāt kvāthaṃ śukākhyasvarasaṃ tathā| eṣa
            kṣāras tu pānīyaḥ ślīpadaṃ hanti sevitaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.66"> apacīṃ galagaṇḍaṃ ca grahaṇīdoṣam eva ca|
            bhaktasyānaśanaṃ caiva hanyāt sarvaviṣāṇi ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.67"> eṣveva tailaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ nasyābhyaṅgeṣu pūjitam|
            etānevāmayān hanti ye ca duṣṭavraṇā nṛṇām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.68"> dravantīṃ trivṛtāṃ dantīṃ nīlīṃ śyāmāṃ tathaiva ca|
            saptalāṃ śaṅkhinīṃ caiva dagdhvā mūtreṇa gālayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.69"> dadyāc ca triphalākvāthameṣa kṣāras tu sādhitaḥ| adho
            gacchati pītas tu pūrvaiś cāpy āśiṣaḥ samāḥ||</l>
          <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsitasthāne vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpaḥ cikitsitaṃ
            nāmaikonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||19||</trailer>
        </div>
        <div n="20" subtype="adhyāya" type="level2">
          <head>viṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ|</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.1"> athātaḥ kṣudrarogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.3"> tatrājagallikāmāmāṃ jalaukobhir upācaret|
            śuktiśrughnīyavakṣārakalkaiś cālepayed bhiṣak|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.4"> śyāmālāṅgalakipāṭhākalkair vā+api vicakṣaṇaḥ| pakvāṃ
            vraṇavidhānena yathoktena prasādhayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.5"> andhālajīṃ yavaprakhyāṃ panasīṃ kacchapīṃ tathā|
            pāṣāṇagardabhaṃ caiva pūrvaṃ svedena yojayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.6"> manaḥśilātālakuṣṭhadārukalkaiḥ pralepayet| paripākagatān
            bhittvā vraṇavat samupācaret|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.7"> vivṛtāmindravṛddhāṃ ca gardabhīṃ jālagardabham| irivellīṃ
            gandhanāmnīṃ kakṣāṃ visphoṭakāṃstathā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.8"> pittajasya visarpasya kriyayā sādhayed bhiṣak| ropayet
            sarpiṣā pakvān siddhena madhurauṣadhaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.9"> cipya(ppa)muṣṇāmbunā siktamutkṛtya srāvayed bhiṣak|
            cakratailena cābhyajya sarjacūrṇena cūrṇayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.10"> bandhenopacareccainamaśakyaṃ cāgninā dahet|
            madhurauṣadhasiddhena tatastailena ropayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.11"> kunakhe vidhirapyeṣa kāryo hi bhiṣajā bhavet| upācared
            anuśayīṃ śleṣmavidradhivadbhiṣak|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.12"> vidārikāṃ samabhyajya svinnāṃ vimlāpya lepayet|
            nagavṛttikavarṣābhūbilvamūlaiḥ supeṣitaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.13"> vraṇabhāvagatāyāṃ vā kṛtvā saṃśodhanakriyām| ropaṇārthaṃ
            hitaṃ tailaṃ kaṣāyamadhuraiḥ śṛtam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.14"> pracchānair vā jalaukobhiḥ srāvyā+apakvā vidārikā|
            ajakarṇaiḥ sapālāśamūlakalkaiḥ pralepayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.15"> pakvāṃ vidārya śastreṇa paṭolapicumardayoḥ| kalkena
            tilayuktena sarpirmiśreṇa lepayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.16"> vaddhvā ca kṣīravṛkṣasya kaṣāyaiḥ khadirasya ca| vraṇaṃ
            prakṣālayec chuddhāṃ tatastāṃ ropayet punaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.17"> medo 'rbudavidhānena sādhayec charkarārbudam| kacchūṃ
            vicarcikāṃ pāmāṃ kuṣṭhavat samupācaret|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.18"> lepaś ca śasyate sikthaśatāhvāgaurasarṣapaiḥ|
            vacādārvīsarṣapair vā tailaṃ vā naktamālajam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.19"> sāratailamathābhyaṅge kurvīta kaṭukaiḥ śṛtam| pādadāryāṃ
            sirāṃ viddhvā svedābhyaṅgau prayojayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.20"> madhūcchiṣṭavasāmajjasarjacūrṇaghṛtaiḥ kṛtaḥ|
            yavāhvagairikonmiśraiḥ pādalepaḥ praśasyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.21"> pādau siktvā++āranālena lepanaṃ hy alase hitam|
            kalkīkṛtairnimbatilakāsīsālaiḥ sasaindhavaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.22"> lākṣāraso 'bhayā vā+api kāryaṃ syādraktamokṣaṇam|
            siddhaṃ rase kaṇṭakāryāstailaṃ vā sārṣapaṃ hitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.23"> kāsīsarocanaśilācūrṇair vā pratisāraṇam| utkṛtya dagdhvā
            snehena jayet kadarasaṃjñakam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.24"> indralupte sirāṃ mūrdhni snigdhasvinnasya mokṣayet|
            kalkaiḥ samaricairdihyācchilākāsīsatutthakaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.25"> kaṭannaṭadārukalkairlepanaṃ vā praśasyate|
            pracchayitvā+avagāḍhaṃ vā guñjākalkairmuhurmuhuḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.26"> lepayed upaśāntyarthaṃ kuryād vā+api rasāyanam|
            mālatīkaravīrāgninaktamālavipācitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.27"> tailamabhyañjane śastamindraluptāpahaṃ param| arūṃṣikāṃ
            hṛte rakte secayennimbavāriṇā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.28"> dihyāt saindhavayuktena vājiviṣṭhārasena tu|
            haritālaniśānimbakalkair vā sapaṭolajaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.29"> yaṣṭīnīlotpalairaṇḍamārkavair vā pralepayet|
            indraluptāpahaṃ tailamabhyaṅge ca praśasyate| sirāṃ dāruṇake viddhvā
            snigdhasvinnasya mūrdhani|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.30"> avapīḍaṃ śirobastimabhyaṅgaṃ ca prayojayet| kṣālane
            kodravatṛṇakṣāratoyaṃ praśasyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.31"> upariṣṭāt rpavakṣyāmi vidhiṃ palitanāśanam| masūrikāyāṃ
            kuṣṭhaghnalepanādikriyā hitā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.32"> pittaśleṣmavisarpoktā kriyā vā saṃpraśasyate| jatumaṇiṃ
            samutkṛtya maṣakaṃ tilakālakam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.33"> kṣāreṇa pradahed yuktyā vahninā vā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ|
            nyacche vyaṅge sirāmokṣo nīlikāyāṃ ca śasyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.34"> yathānyāyaṃ yathābhyāsaṃ lālāṭyādisirāvyadhaḥ| ghṛṣṭvā
            dihyāttvacaṃ piṣṭvā kṣīriṇāṃ kṣīrasaṃyutām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.35"> balatibalayaṣṭyāhvarajanīrvā pralepanam|
            payasyāgurukālīyalepanaṃ vā sagairikam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.36"> kṣaudrājyayuktayā limped daṃṣṭrayā śūkarasya ca|
            kapittharājādanayoḥ kalkaṃ vā hitamucyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.37"> yauvane piḍakāsveṣa viśeṣācchardanaṃ hitam| lepanaṃ ca
            vacārodhrasaindhavaiḥ sarṣapānvitaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38"> kustumburuvacālodhrakuṣṭharvā lepanaṃ hitam|
            padminīkaṇṭake roge chardayennimbavāriṇā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.39"> tenaiva siddhaṃ sakṣaudraṃ sarpiḥpānaṃ pradāpayet|
            nimbāragvadhayoḥ kalko hita utsādane bhavet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.40"> parivṛttiṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ susvinnām upanāhayet| tato
            'bhyajya śanaiścarma cānayet pīḍayenmaṇim|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.41"> praviṣṭe ca maṇau carma svedayed upanāhanaiḥ| trirātraṃ
            pañcarātraṃ vā vātaghnaiḥ sālvaṇādibhiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.42"> dadyādvātaharān bastīn snigdhānyannāni bhojayet |
            vapāṭikāṃ jayed evaṃ yathādoṣaṃ cikitsakaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.43"> niruddhaprakaśe nāḍīṃ lauhīmubhayatomukhīm| dāravīṃ vā
            jatukṛtāṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ praveśayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.44"> pariṣeke vasāmajjaśiśumāravarāhayoḥ| cakratailaṃ tathā
            yojyaṃ vātaghnadravyasaṃyutam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.45"> tryahāttryahāt sthūlatarāṃ samyaṅnāḍīṃ praveśayet| sroto
            vivardhayed evaṃ snigdhamannaṃ ca bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.46"> bhittvā vā sevanīṃ muktvā sadyaḥkṣatavadācaret|
            sanniruddhagudaṃ rogaṃ valmīkaṃ vahnirohiṇīm|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.47"> pratyākhyāya yathāyogaṃ cikitsitamathācaret|
            visarpoktena vidhinā sādhayed agnirohiṇīm|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.48"> sanniruddhagude yojyā niruddhaprakaśakriyā|
            śastreṇotkṛtya valmīkaṃ kṣārāgnibhyāṃ prasādhayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.49"> vidhānenārbudoktena śodhayitvā ca ropayet| valmīkaṃ tu
            bhaved yasya nātivṛddhamamarmajam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.50"> tatra saṃśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śoṇitaṃ mokṣayed bhiṣak|
            kulatthikāyā mūlaiś ca guḍūcyā lavaṇena ca|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.51"> ārevatasya mūlaiśca dantīmūlais tathaiva ca| śyāmāmūlaiḥ
            sapalalaiḥ śaktumiśraiḥ pralepayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.52"> susnigdhaiś ca sukhoṣṇaiśca bhiṣak tam upanāhayet|
            pakvaṃ vā tadvijānīyād gatīḥ sarvā yathākramam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.53"> abhijñāya tataśchittvā pradahenmatimān bhiṣak| saṃśodhya
            duṣṭamāṃsāni kṣāreṇa pratisārayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.54"> vraṇaṃ viśuddhaṃ vijñāya ropayenmatimān bhiṣak| sumanā
            granthayaś caiva bhallātakamanaḥśile|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.55"> kālānusārī sūkṣmailā candanāguruṇī tathā| etaiḥ siddhaṃ
            nimbatailaṃ valmīke ropaṇaṃ hitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.56"> pāṇipādopariṣṭāttu chidrairbahubhir āvṛtam| valmīkaṃ yat
            saśophaṃ syādvarjyaṃ tat tu vijānatā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.57"> dhātryāḥ stanyaṃ śodhayitvā bāle sādhyā+ahipūtanā|
            paṭolapatratriphalārasāñjanavipācitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.58"> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ nāśayati kṛcchrāmapyahipūtanām|
            triphalākolakhadirakaṣāyaṃ vraṇaropaṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.59"> kāsīsarocanātutthaharitālarasāñjanaiḥ| lepo 'mlapiṣṭo
            badarītvagvā saindhavasaṃyutā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.60"> kapālatutthajaṃ cūrṇaṃ cūrṇakāle prayojayet|
            cikitsenmuṣkakacchūṃ cāpy ahipūtanapāmavat|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.61"> gudabhraṃśe gudaṃ svinnaṃ snehābhyaktaṃ praveśayet|
            kārayed gophaṇābandhaṃ madhyacchidreṇa carmaṇā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.62"> vinirgamārthaṃ vāyośca svedayec ca muhurmuhuḥ| kṣīre
            mahatpañcamūlaṃ mūṣikāṃ cāntravarjitām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.63"> paktvā tasmin pacetailaṃ vātaghnauṣadhasaṃyutam|
            gudabhraṃśamidaṃ kṛcchraṃ pānābhyaṅgāt prasādhayet||</l>
          <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne kṣudrarogacikitsitaṃ nāma viṃśo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||20||</trailer>
        </div>
      </div>


    </body>
